<!-- JavaScript Calculator Logic -->
<script>
let cart = [];

// Format rupiah
function formatRupiah(amount) {
    return new Intl.NumberFormat('id-ID', {
        style: 'currency',
        currency: 'IDR',
        minimumFractionDigits: 0
    }).format(amount);
}

// Toggle service selection
function toggleService(element) {
    const id = element.dataset.id;
    const name = element.dataset.name;
    const price = parseFloat(element.dataset.price);
    
    const index = cart.findIndex(item => item.id === id);
    
    if (index > -1) {
        // Remove from cart
        cart.splice(index, 1);
        element.classList.remove('selected');
    } else {
        // Add to cart
        cart.push({ id, name, price });
        element.classList.add('selected');
    }
    
    updateCart();
}

// Update cart display
function updateCart() {
    const cartItemsDiv = document.getElementById('cartItems');
    const cartSummaryDiv = document.getElementById('cartSummary');
    const selectedCount = document.getElementById('selectedCount');
    
    // Update count
    selectedCount.textContent = cart.length + ' <?php echo $t['selected']; ?>';
    
    if (cart.length === 0) {
        cartItemsDiv.innerHTML = `
            <div class="empty-cart">
                <i class="bi bi-cart-x"></i>
                <p class="text-light"><?php echo $t['empty_cart']; ?></p>
            </div>
        `;
        cartSummaryDiv.style.display = 'none';
        return;
    }
    
    // Show cart items
    let itemsHTML = '';
    cart.forEach((item, index) => {
        itemsHTML += `
            <div class="cart-item">
                <div>
                    <div class="text-gold fw-semibold">${item.name}</div>
                    <small class="text-light">${formatRupiah(item.price)}</small>
                </div>
                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-danger" onclick="removeItem(${index})">
                    <i class="bi bi-trash"></i>
                </button>
            </div>
        `;
    });
    
    cartItemsDiv.innerHTML = itemsHTML;
    cartSummaryDiv.style.display = 'block';
    
    // Calculate totals
    const subtotal = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.price, 0);
    let discountPercent = 0;
    
    // Apply discount rules
    if (cart.length >= 5) {
        discountPercent = <?php echo DISCOUNT_5_SERVICES; ?>;
    } else if (cart.length >= 3) {
        discountPercent = <?php echo DISCOUNT_3_SERVICES; ?>;
    }
    
    const discountAmount = subtotal * (discountPercent / 100);
    const total = subtotal - discountAmount;
    
    // Update display
    document.getElementById('subtotalAmount').textContent = formatRupiah(subtotal);
    document.getElementById('totalAmount').textContent = formatRupiah(total);
    
    // Show/hide discount
    const discountRow = document.getElementById('discountRow');
    const discountInfo = document.getElementById('discountInfo');
    
    if (discountPercent > 0) {
        discountRow.style.display = 'flex';
        discountInfo.style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById('discountPercent').textContent = discountPercent;
        document.getElementById('discountAmount').textContent = formatRupiah(discountAmount);
        
        let discountText = '';
        if (cart.length >= 5) {
            discountText = '<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Selamat! Kamu dapat diskon 15%" : "Congratulations! You get 15% discount"; ?>';
        } else if (cart.length >= 3) {
            discountText = '<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Selamat! Kamu dapat diskon 10%. Tambah 2 layanan lagi untuk diskon 15%!" : "Congratulations! You get 10% discount. Add 2 more services for 15% discount!"; ?>';
        }
        document.getElementById('discountText').textContent = discountText;
    } else {
        discountRow.style.display = 'none';
        discountInfo.style.display = 'none';
    }
}

// Remove item from cart
function removeItem(index) {
    const item = cart[index];
    const card = document.querySelector(`[data-id="${item.id}"]`);
    if (card) {
        card.classList.remove('selected');
    }
    cart.splice(index, 1);
    updateCart();
}

// Clear cart
function clearCart() {
    if (confirm('<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Yakin mau hapus semua?" : "Are you sure you want to clear all?"; ?>')) {
        document.querySelectorAll('.service-select-card.selected').forEach(card => {
            card.classList.remove('selected');
        });
        cart = [];
        updateCart();
    }
}

// Order now
function orderNow() {
    if (cart.length === 0) {
        alert('<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Pilih layanan dulu ya!" : "Please select services first!"; ?>');
        return;
    }
    
    const subtotal = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.price, 0);
    let discountPercent = 0;
    
    if (cart.length >= 5) {
        discountPercent = <?php echo DISCOUNT_5_SERVICES; ?>;
    } else if (cart.length >= 3) {
        discountPercent = <?php echo DISCOUNT_3_SERVICES; ?>;
    }
    
    const discountAmount = subtotal * (discountPercent / 100);
    const total = subtotal - discountAmount;
    
    let message = '<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "*PESANAN DARI CALCULATOR*" : "*ORDER FROM CALCULATOR*"; ?>\n\n';
    message += '<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Halo Situneo! Saya mau pesan layanan berikut:" : "Hello Situneo! I want to order the following services:"; ?>\n\n';
    
    cart.forEach((item, index) => {
        message += `${index + 1}. ${item.name} - ${formatRupiah(item.price)}\n`;
    });
    
    message += '\n<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "RINGKASAN:" : "SUMMARY:"; ?>\n';
    message += `Subtotal: ${formatRupiah(subtotal)}\n`;
    
    if (discountPercent > 0) {
        message += `<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Diskon" : "Discount"; ?> (${discountPercent}%): -${formatRupiah(discountAmount)}\n`;
    }
    
    message += `*TOTAL: ${formatRupiah(total)}*\n\n`;
    message += '<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Mohon info lebih lanjut ya! üôè" : "Please provide more information! üôè"; ?>';
    
    const waURL = '<?php echo getWhatsAppURL(""); ?>'.replace(/text=.*$/, 'text=' + encodeURIComponent(message));
    window.open(waURL, '_blank');
}

// Share to WhatsApp
function shareWhatsApp() {
    orderNow(); // Same as order now
}

// Initialize with pre-selected service
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    <?php if ($preSelectService): ?>
    const preSelectedCard = document.querySelector('[data-id="<?php echo $preSelectService; ?>"]');
    if (preSelectedCard) {
        toggleService(preSelectedCard);
    }
    <?php endif; ?>
});
</script>

<?php include 'includes/footer.php'; ?>
```

<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Contact Page
 * File: contact.php
 * Purpose: Contact form + info lengkap
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once 'includes/config.php';
require_once 'includes/functions.php';

// Handle language switch
if (isset($_GET['lang']) && in_array($_GET['lang'], AVAILABLE_LANGS)) {
    setCurrentLang($_GET['lang']);
    redirect('contact.php');
}

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();

// Handle form submission
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['submit_contact'])) {
    $name = cleanInput($_POST['name'] ?? '');
    $email = cleanInput($_POST['email'] ?? '');
    $phone = cleanInput($_POST['phone'] ?? '');
    $subject = cleanInput($_POST['subject'] ?? '');
    $message = cleanInput($_POST['message'] ?? '');
    
    $errors = [];
    
    // Validation
    if (empty($name)) {
        $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Nama harus diisi!' : 'Name is required!';
    }
    
    if (empty($email) || !isValidEmail($email)) {
        $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Email tidak valid!' : 'Invalid email!';
    }
    
    if (empty($phone) || !isValidPhone($phone)) {
        $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Nomor HP tidak valid!' : 'Invalid phone number!';
    }
    
    if (empty($message)) {
        $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Pesan harus diisi!' : 'Message is required!';
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        // Save to database (optional - buat table contact_messages kalau mau)
        // For now, just send email atau redirect ke WhatsApp
        
        $waMessage = "*KONTAK DARI WEBSITE*\n\n";
        $waMessage .= "Nama: {$name}\n";
        $waMessage .= "Email: {$email}\n";
        $waMessage .= "HP: {$phone}\n";
        if ($subject) {
            $waMessage .= "Subjek: {$subject}\n";
        }
        $waMessage .= "\nPesan:\n{$message}";
        
        setFlashMessage('success', $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Pesan berhasil dikirim! Kami akan segera menghubungi Anda.' : 'Message sent successfully! We will contact you soon.');
        
        // Redirect ke WhatsApp
        $waURL = getWhatsAppURL($waMessage);
        header("Location: {$waURL}");
        exit();
    } else {
        foreach($errors as $error) {
            setFlashMessage('error', $error);
        }
    }
}

// Translations

### **1Ô∏è‚É£ Upload ke Hosting (cPanel):**

```
üìÅ public_html/
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ üìÅ includes/
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ config.php

‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ üìÅ uploads/ (buat folder ini, chmod 755)
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ üìÅ assets/ (kalau ada CSS/JS tambahan)
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ index.php
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ about.php

‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ pricing.php
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ calculator.php
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ contact.php
```

### **2Ô∏è‚É£ Import Database:**
1. Buka **phpMyAdmin** di cPanel
2. Buat database baru: `situneo_db`
3. Import file **situneo.sql**
4. User akan otomatis ter-create

### **3Ô∏è‚É£ Edit Config File:**

Buka `includes/config.php` dan edit:

```php
// Line 28-31
define('DB_HOST', 'localhost');        
define('DB_USER', 'username_db_kamu'); // Ganti!
define('DB_PASS', 'password_db_kamu'); // Ganti!
define('DB_NAME', 'situneo_db');       

// Line 40
define('SITE_URL', 'https://situneo.my.id'); // Ganti dengan domain kamu!
```

### **4Ô∏è‚É£ Set Permissions:**

Via cPanel File Manager atau FTP:
```bash
chmod 755 uploads/
chmod 644 *.php
chmod 644 includes/*.php
```

### **5Ô∏è‚É£ Test Website:**

Buka browser: `https://domainanda.com`

**Login Default:**
- Email: `admin@situneo.my.id`
- Password: `Situneo2025`

## üêõ **TROUBLESHOOTING:**

### **Error: Database Connection Failed**
```php
// Check config.php line 28-31
// Pastikan DB_USER, DB_PASS, DB_NAME sudah benar
```

### **Error: 500 Internal Server Error**
```php
// Edit config.php line 222-223
error_reporting(E_ALL);
ini_set('display_errors', 1);
// Lihat error message-nya
```

### **Images/Upload Not Working**
```bash
# Via terminal atau cPanel
chmod 755 uploads/
chown username:username uploads/
```

### **WhatsApp Link Not Working**
```php
// Check config.php line 68
define('CONTACT_WHATSAPP', '6283173868915'); // Harus pakai 62, tanpa +
```

## üìñ **DOKUMENTASI FUNGSI PENTING:**

### **Helper Functions (functions.php):**

```php
// User Management
isLoggedIn()              // Check if user logged in
hasRole('admin')          // Check user role
loginUser($userData)      // Login user
logoutUser()             // Logout user

// Database Queries
getServices($filters)     // Get services with filters
getService($id)          // Get single service
getPackages()            // Get all packages
getPortfolios()          // Get portfolios
getTestimonials()        // Get testimonials

// Formatting
formatRupiah(350000)     // Output: Rp 350.000
formatTanggal('2025-01-01')  // Output: 01 Jan 2025
cleanInput($data)        // Sanitize input (XSS protection)

// Orders
createOrder($userId, $items, $referralCode)  // Create new order
getUserOrders($userId)   // Get user's orders

// Utilities
getWhatsAppURL($message) // Generate WhatsApp URL
setFlashMessage('success', 'Pesan berhasil!')
redirect('index.php')    // Redirect ke halaman lain
```

## üí° **TIPS & BEST PRACTICES:**

```php
// SELALU sanitize input
$name = cleanInput($_POST['name']);

// SELALU validate
if (!isValidEmail($email)) {
    // Handle error
}

// JANGAN tampilkan error detail di production
error_reporting(0); // Set di config.php line 222
```

### **2. Performance:**
```php
// Gunakan lazy loading untuk images
<img src="image.jpg" loading="lazy">

// Limit database queries
$services = getServices([], 10); // Limit 10
```

## üîê **MULAI DARI AUTH SYSTEM!**

### **FILE 1: auth/login.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Login Page
 * File: auth/login.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

// Redirect kalau udah login
if (isLoggedIn()) {
    $role = $_SESSION['user_role'];
    if ($role === 'admin') {
        redirect('../admin/index.php');
    } elseif ($role === 'freelancer') {
        redirect('../freelance/index.php');
    } else {
        redirect('../client/index.php');
    }
}

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();

// Handle login submission
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['login'])) {
    $email = cleanInput($_POST['email'] ?? '');
    $password = $_POST['password'] ?? '';
    $remember = isset($_POST['remember']);
    
    $errors = [];
    
    // Validation
    if (empty($email) || !isValidEmail($email)) {
        $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Email tidak valid!' : 'Invalid email!';
    }
    
    if (empty($password)) {
        $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Password harus diisi!' : 'Password is required!';
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        // Check user di database
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = ? AND status = 'active'");
        $stmt->execute([$email]);
        $user = $stmt->fetch();
        
        if ($user && password_verify($password, $user['password'])) {
            // Login success
            loginUser($user);
            
            // Remember me
            if ($remember) {
                // Set cookie untuk 30 hari
                setcookie('remember_token', base64_encode($user['user_id']), time() + (86400 * 30), '/');
            }
            
            // Redirect based on role
            if ($user['role'] === 'admin') {
                setFlashMessage('success', $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Selamat datang Admin!' : 'Welcome Admin!');
                redirect('../admin/index.php');
            } elseif ($user['role'] === 'freelancer') {
                setFlashMessage('success', $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Selamat datang Freelancer!' : 'Welcome Freelancer!');
                redirect('../freelance/index.php');
            } else {
                setFlashMessage('success', $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Login berhasil!' : 'Login successful!');
                redirect('../client/index.php');
            }
        } else {
            $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Email atau password salah!' : 'Invalid email or password!';
        }
    }
    
    if (!empty($errors)) {
        foreach($errors as $error) {
            setFlashMessage('error', $error);
        }
    }
}

$text = [
    'id' => [
        'page_title' => 'Login',
        'title' => 'Masuk ke Akun Anda',
        'subtitle' => 'Belum punya akun?',
        'register_link' => 'Daftar Sekarang',
        'email_label' => 'Email',
        'password_label' => 'Password',
        'remember_me' => 'Ingat Saya',
        'forgot_password' => 'Lupa Password?',
        'login_btn' => 'MASUK',
        'or_login_with' => 'Atau masuk dengan',
        'back_home' => 'Kembali ke Beranda'
    ],
    'en' => [
        'page_title' => 'Login',
        'title' => 'Login to Your Account',
        'subtitle' => 'Don\'t have an account?',
        'register_link' => 'Register Now',
        'email_label' => 'Email',
        'password_label' => 'Password',
        'remember_me' => 'Remember Me',
        'forgot_password' => 'Forgot Password?',
        'login_btn' => 'LOGIN',
        'or_login_with' => 'Or login with',
        'back_home' => 'Back to Home'
    ]
];

$t = $text[$currentLang];
$pageTitle = $t['page_title'] . ' - ' . SITE_NAME;
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<style>
body {
    background: linear-gradient(135deg, #0F3057 0%, #000000 100%);
    min-height: 100vh;
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    padding: 2rem;
}

.login-container {
    max-width: 450px;
    width: 100%;
}

.login-card {
    background: linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(30,92,153,0.2) 0%, rgba(15,48,87,0.3) 100%);
    border: 2px solid rgba(255,180,0,0.3);
    border-radius: 30px;
    padding: 3rem;
    backdrop-filter: blur(20px);
    box-shadow: 0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.5);
}

.login-logo {
    text-align: center;
    margin-bottom: 2rem;
}

.login-logo img {
    width: 80px;
    height: 80px;
    border-radius: 20px;
    box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(255,180,0,0.4);
    margin-bottom: 1rem;
}

.form-control-auth {
    background: rgba(255,255,255,0.05);
    border: 2px solid rgba(255,180,0,0.3);
    border-radius: 15px;
    color: white;
    padding: 15px 20px;
    transition: all 0.3s;
}

.form-control-auth:focus {
    background: rgba(255,255,255,0.1);
    border-color: var(--gold);
    box-shadow: 0 0 0 0.25rem rgba(255, 180, 0, 0.25);
    color: white;
}

.form-control-auth::placeholder {
    color: rgba(255,255,255,0.5);
}

.form-check-input {
    background-color: rgba(255,255,255,0.1);
    border-color: rgba(255,180,0,0.5);
}

.form-check-input:checked {
    background-color: var(--gold);
    border-color: var(--gold);
}

.divider {
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    text-align: center;
    margin: 1.5rem 0;
}

.divider::before,
.divider::after {
    content: '';
    flex: 1;
    border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,180,0,0.3);
}

.divider span {
    padding: 0 1rem;
    color: var(--text-light);
    font-size: 0.9rem;
}
</style>

<div class="login-container" data-aos="zoom-in">
    <div class="login-card">
        <!-- Logo -->

<script>
function togglePassword() {
    const passwordInput = document.getElementById('password');
    const toggleIcon = document.getElementById('toggleIcon');
    
    if (passwordInput.type === 'password') {
        passwordInput.type = 'text';
        toggleIcon.classList.remove('bi-eye');
        toggleIcon.classList.add('bi-eye-slash');
    } else {
        passwordInput.type = 'password';
        toggleIcon.classList.remove('bi-eye-slash');
        toggleIcon.classList.add('bi-eye');
    }
}

// Auto-hide flash messages
setTimeout(() => {
    const flashMessages = document.querySelectorAll('.flash-message');
    flashMessages.forEach(msg => {
        msg.style.opacity = '0';
        setTimeout(() => msg.remove(), 300);
    });
}, 5000);
</script>

<!-- Load AOS -->
<script src="https://unpkg.com/aos@2.3.1/dist/aos.js"></script>
<script>
    AOS.init({
        duration: 800,
        once: true
    });
</script>

<!-- Load Bootstrap JS -->
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.3/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>

</body>
</html>

### **FILE 2: auth/register.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Register Page
 * File: auth/register.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

// Redirect kalau udah login
if (isLoggedIn()) {
    redirect('../client/index.php');
}

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();

// Handle registration
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['register'])) {
    $fullName = cleanInput($_POST['full_name'] ?? '');
    $email = cleanInput($_POST['email'] ?? '');
    $phone = cleanInput($_POST['phone'] ?? '');
    $password = $_POST['password'] ?? '';
    $confirmPassword = $_POST['confirm_password'] ?? '';
    $role = cleanInput($_POST['role'] ?? 'client');
    $referralCode = cleanInput($_POST['referral_code'] ?? '');
    $agreeTerms = isset($_POST['agree_terms']);
    
    $errors = [];
    
    // Validation
    if (empty($fullName) || strlen($fullName) < 3) {
        $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Nama minimal 3 karakter!' : 'Name minimum 3 characters!';
    }
    
    if (empty($email) || !isValidEmail($email)) {
        $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Email tidak valid!' : 'Invalid email!';
    }
    
    if (empty($phone) || !isValidPhone($phone)) {
        $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Nomor HP tidak valid!' : 'Invalid phone number!';
    }
    
    $passwordValidation = validatePassword($password);
    if (!$passwordValidation['valid']) {
        $errors[] = $passwordValidation['message'];
    }
    
    if ($password !== $confirmPassword) {
        $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Password tidak cocok!' : 'Passwords do not match!';
    }
    
    if (!$agreeTerms) {
        $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Anda harus setuju dengan syarat & ketentuan!' : 'You must agree to terms & conditions!';
    }
    
    // Check email exists
    if (empty($errors)) {
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT user_id FROM users WHERE email = ?");
        $stmt->execute([$email]);
        if ($stmt->fetch()) {
            $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Email sudah terdaftar!' : 'Email already registered!';
        }
    }
    
    // Validate referral code kalau jadi freelancer
    if ($role === 'freelancer' && !empty($referralCode)) {
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT user_id FROM users WHERE referral_code = ?");
        $stmt->execute([$referralCode]);
        if ($stmt->fetch()) {
            $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Kode referral sudah digunakan!' : 'Referral code already used!';
        }
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        try {
            // Hash password
            $hashedPassword = password_hash($password, PASSWORD_DEFAULT);
            
            // Generate referral code kalau freelancer
            $userReferralCode = null;
            if ($role === 'freelancer') {
                $userReferralCode = $referralCode ?: strtoupper(generateRandomString(8));
            }
            
            // Insert user
            $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                INSERT INTO users (email, password, full_name, phone, role, referral_code, status, email_verified)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 'active', 0)
            ");
            $stmt->execute([
                $email,
                $hashedPassword,
                $fullName,
                $phone,
                $role,
                $userReferralCode
            ]);
            
            // Send welcome email (optional)
            sendWelcomeEmail($email, $fullName);
            
            // Auto login
            $userId = $pdo->lastInsertId();
            $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM users WHERE user_id = ?");
            $stmt->execute([$userId]);
            $user = $stmt->fetch();
            
            loginUser($user);
            
            setFlashMessage('success', $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Registrasi berhasil! Selamat datang!' : 'Registration successful! Welcome!');
            
            // Redirect based on role
            if ($role === 'freelancer') {
                redirect('../freelance/index.php');
            } else {
                redirect('../client/index.php');
            }
            
        } catch (Exception $e) {
            error_log("Registration Error: " . $e->getMessage());
            $errors[] = $currentLang == 'id' ? 'Terjadi kesalahan. Silakan coba lagi.' : 'An error occurred. Please try again.';
        }
    }
    
    if (!empty($errors)) {
        foreach($errors as $error) {
            setFlashMessage('error', $error);
        }
    }
}

$text = [
    'id' => [
        'page_title' => 'Daftar',
        'title' => 'Buat Akun Baru',
        'subtitle' => 'Sudah punya akun?',
        'login_link' => 'Masuk Sekarang',
        'full_name' => 'Nama Lengkap',
        'email' => 'Email',
        'phone' => 'Nomor HP',
        'password' => 'Password',
        'confirm_password' => 'Konfirmasi Password',
        'register_as' => 'Daftar Sebagai',
        'client' => 'Client (Pemesan)',
        'freelancer' => 'Freelancer (Referral)',
        'referral_code' => 'Kode Referral (Optional)',
        'agree_terms' => 'Saya setuju dengan',
        'terms_link' => 'Syarat & Ketentuan',
        'register_btn' => 'DAFTAR SEKARANG',
        'back_home' => 'Kembali ke Beranda'
    ],
    'en' => [
        'page_title' => 'Register',
        'title' => 'Create New Account',
        'subtitle' => 'Already have an account?',
        'login_link' => 'Login Now',
        'full_name' => 'Full Name',
        'email' => 'Email',
        'phone' => 'Phone Number',
        'password' => 'Password',
        'confirm_password' => 'Confirm Password',
        'register_as' => 'Register As',
        'client' => 'Client (Customer)',
        'freelancer' => 'Freelancer (Referral)',
        'referral_code' => 'Referral Code (Optional)',
        'agree_terms' => 'I agree to',
        'terms_link' => 'Terms & Conditions',
        'register_btn' => 'REGISTER NOW',
        'back_home' => 'Back to Home'
    ]
];

$t = $text[$currentLang];
$pageTitle = $t['page_title'] . ' - ' . SITE_NAME;
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<script>
function toggleReferralCode() {
    const roleSelect = document.getElementById('roleSelect');
    const referralCodeDiv = document.getElementById('referralCodeDiv');
    
    if (roleSelect.value === 'freelancer') {
        referralCodeDiv.style.display = 'block';
    } else {
        referralCodeDiv.style.display = 'none';
    }
}

function checkPasswordStrength(password) {
    const strengthBar = document.getElementById('strengthBar');
    const strengthText = document.getElementById('strengthText');


Áî®Êà∑:
Continue

Claude:
```javascript
    
    let strength = 0;
    let text = '';
    
    // Check password length
    if (password.length >= 8) strength++;
    if (password.length >= 12) strength++;
    
    // Check for numbers
    if (/\d/.test(password)) strength++;
    
    // Check for lowercase and uppercase
    if (/[a-z]/.test(password) && /[A-Z]/.test(password)) strength++;
    
    // Check for special characters
    if (/[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(password)) strength++;
    
    // Set strength bar
    strengthBar.className = 'password-strength-bar';
    
    if (strength <= 2) {
        strengthBar.classList.add('weak');
        text = '<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Lemah" : "Weak"; ?>';
    } else if (strength <= 4) {
        strengthBar.classList.add('medium');
        text = '<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Sedang" : "Medium"; ?>';
    } else {
        strengthBar.classList.add('strong');
        text = '<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Kuat" : "Strong"; ?>';
    }
    
    strengthText.textContent = text;
}

// Auto-hide flash messages
setTimeout(() => {
    const flashMessages = document.querySelectorAll('.flash-message');
    flashMessages.forEach(msg => {
        msg.style.opacity = '0';
        setTimeout(() => msg.remove(), 300);
    });
}, 5000);
</script>

/**
 * =====================================================

 * File: auth/logout.php

## üéõÔ∏è **DASHBOARD FILES!**

### **FILE 4: admin/index.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Admin Dashboard
 * File: admin/index.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

// Require admin role
requireRole('admin');

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();

// Get dashboard stats
$stats = [];

// Total users by role
$stmt = $pdo->query("
    SELECT role, COUNT(*) as count 
    FROM users 
    WHERE status = 'active'
    GROUP BY role
");
while ($row = $stmt->fetch()) {
    $stats['users_' . $row['role']] = $row['count'];
}

// Total orders
$stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM orders");
$stats['total_orders'] = $stmt->fetch()['count'];

// Pending orders
$stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM orders WHERE status = 'pending'");
$stats['pending_orders'] = $stmt->fetch()['count'];

// Total revenue
$stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT SUM(final_amount) as total FROM orders WHERE status IN ('paid', 'completed')");
$stats['total_revenue'] = $stmt->fetch()['total'] ?? 0;

// Revenue this month
$stmt = $pdo->query("
    SELECT SUM(final_amount) as total 
    FROM orders 
    WHERE status IN ('paid', 'completed') 
    AND MONTH(created_at) = MONTH(CURRENT_DATE())
    AND YEAR(created_at) = YEAR(CURRENT_DATE())
");
$stats['revenue_this_month'] = $stmt->fetch()['total'] ?? 0;

// Recent orders
$stmt = $pdo->query("
    SELECT o.*, u.full_name 
    FROM orders o
    LEFT JOIN users u ON o.user_id = u.user_id
    ORDER BY o.created_at DESC
    LIMIT 10
");
$recentOrders = $stmt->fetchAll();

// Recent users
$stmt = $pdo->query("
    SELECT * FROM users 
    ORDER BY created_at DESC
    LIMIT 5
");
$recentUsers = $stmt->fetchAll();

$pageTitle = 'Admin Dashboard - ' . SITE_NAME;
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<style>
body {
    background: var(--bg-dark);
}

    display: flex;

    padding: 2rem 0;
    position: fixed;
    height: 100vh;
    overflow-y: auto;
    backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
}

.sidebar-brand {
    padding: 0 1.5rem 2rem;
    text-align: center;
    border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,180,0,0.2);
    margin-bottom: 2rem;
}

    width: 60px;
    height: 60px;
    border-radius: 15px;
    margin-bottom: 0.5rem;
}

.sidebar-menu {
    list-style: none;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
}

.sidebar-menu li a {
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    padding: 1rem 1.5rem;
    color: var(--text-light);
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: all 0.3s;
}

.sidebar-menu li a:hover,
.sidebar-menu li a.active {
    background: rgba(255,180,0,0.1);
    color: var(--gold);
    border-left: 4px solid var(--gold);
}

    font-size: 1.2rem;

/* Main Content */
.main-content {
    flex: 1;
    margin-left: 280px;
    padding: 2rem;
}

### **FILE 5: client/index.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Client Dashboard
 * File: client/index.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

// Require client or admin role
requireLogin();

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Get user data
$currentUser = getCurrentUser();

// Get user orders
$userOrders = getUserOrders($userId);

// Calculate stats
$totalOrders = count($userOrders);
$pendingOrders = count(array_filter($userOrders, fn($o) => $o['status'] === 'pending'));
$completedOrders = count(array_filter($userOrders, fn($o) => $o['status'] === 'completed'));
$totalSpent = array_sum(array_map(fn($o) => $o['final_amount'], array_filter($userOrders, fn($o) => $o['status'] !== 'cancelled')));

$pageTitle = 'My Dashboard - ' . SITE_NAME;
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

### **FILE 6: freelance/index.php**

<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Freelancer Dashboard
 * File: freelance/index.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

// Require freelancer role
requireRole('freelancer');

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Get user data
$currentUser = getCurrentUser();

// Get referral code
$referralCode = $currentUser['referral_code'];

// Get referral stats
$stmt = $pdo->prepare("
    SELECT COUNT(*) as total_referrals, SUM(final_amount) as total_sales
    FROM orders 
    WHERE referral_code = ? AND status IN ('paid', 'completed')
");
$stmt->execute([$referralCode]);
$referralStats = $stmt->fetch();

// Get commission stats
$stmt = $pdo->prepare("
    SELECT 
        COUNT(*) as total_commissions,
        SUM(commission_amount) as total_earned,
        SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'pending' THEN commission_amount ELSE 0 END) as pending_amount,
        SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'approved' THEN commission_amount ELSE 0 END) as approved_amount,
        SUM(CASE WHEN status = 'paid' THEN commission_amount ELSE 0 END) as paid_amount
    FROM freelancer_commissions
    WHERE freelancer_id = ?
");
$stmt->execute([$userId]);
$commissionStats = $stmt->fetch();

// Get recent referrals
$stmt = $pdo->prepare("
    SELECT o.*, u.full_name 
    FROM orders o
    LEFT JOIN users u ON o.user_id = u.user_id
    WHERE o.referral_code = ?
    ORDER BY o.created_at DESC
    LIMIT 10
");
$stmt->execute([$referralCode]);
$recentReferrals = $stmt->fetchAll();

// Generate referral link
$referralLink = SITE_URL . '?ref=' . $referralCode;

$pageTitle = 'Freelancer Dashboard - ' . SITE_NAME;
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<script>
function copyReferralLink() {
    const linkInput = document.getElementById('referralLink');
    linkInput.select();
    linkInput.setSelectionRange(0, 99999); // For mobile
    
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(linkInput.value).then(() => {
        alert('<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Link berhasil dicopy!" : "Link copied successfully!"; ?>');
    }).catch(err => {
        alert('<?php echo $currentLang == "id" ? "Gagal copy link" : "Failed to copy link"; ?>');
    });
}
</script>

<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.3/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

### **FILE 1: admin/orders.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Admin Orders Management
 * File: admin/orders.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireRole('admin');

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();

// Handle status update
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['update_status'])) {
    $orderId = (int)$_POST['order_id'];
    $newStatus = cleanInput($_POST['status']);
    
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE orders SET status = ?, updated_at = NOW() WHERE order_id = ?");
    if ($stmt->execute([$newStatus, $orderId])) {
        setFlashMessage('success', 'Order status updated successfully!');
    } else {
        setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to update order status!');
    }
    redirect('orders.php');
}

// Get filter
$filterStatus = $_GET['status'] ?? 'all';
$searchQuery = $_GET['search'] ?? '';

// Build query
$sql = "SELECT o.*, u.full_name, u.email FROM orders o LEFT JOIN users u ON o.user_id = u.user_id WHERE 1=1";
$params = [];

if ($filterStatus !== 'all') {
    $sql .= " AND o.status = ?";
    $params[] = $filterStatus;
}

if ($searchQuery) {
    $sql .= " AND (o.order_number LIKE ? OR u.full_name LIKE ? OR u.email LIKE ?)";
    $params[] = "%$searchQuery%";
    $params[] = "%$searchQuery%";
    $params[] = "%$searchQuery%";
}

$sql .= " ORDER BY o.created_at DESC";

$stmt = $pdo->prepare($sql);
$stmt->execute($params);
$orders = $stmt->fetchAll();

// Count by status
$statusCounts = [];
foreach(['pending', 'paid', 'in_progress', 'completed', 'cancelled'] as $status) {
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM orders WHERE status = ?");
    $stmt->execute([$status]);
    $statusCounts[$status] = $stmt->fetch()['count'];
}

$pageTitle = 'Manage Orders - Admin';
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

                    <option value="pending">Pending</option>
                    <option value="paid">Paid</option>
                    <option value="in_progress">In Progress</option>
                    <option value="completed">Completed</option>
                    <option value="cancelled">Cancelled</option>

                </button>
            </div>

    </div>

<script>
function updateStatus(orderId, currentStatus) {
    document.getElementById('modalOrderId').value = orderId;
    document.querySelector('select[name="status"]').value = currentStatus;
    document.getElementById('statusModal').classList.add('active');
}

function closeModal() {
    document.getElementById('statusModal').classList.remove('active');
}

function viewOrder(orderId) {
    // Redirect to order detail page (to be created)
    window.location.href = 'order-detail.php?id=' + orderId;
}
</script>

<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.3/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>
```

### **FILE 2: admin/users.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Admin Users Management
 * File: admin/users.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireRole('admin');

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();

// Handle user status update
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['update_user_status'])) {
    $userId = (int)$_POST['user_id'];
    $newStatus = cleanInput($_POST['status']);
    
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE users SET status = ? WHERE user_id = ?");
    if ($stmt->execute([$newStatus, $userId])) {
        setFlashMessage('success', 'User status updated!');
    } else {
        setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to update user status!');
    }
    redirect('users.php');
}

// Get filter
$filterRole = $_GET['role'] ?? 'all';
$filterStatus = $_GET['status'] ?? 'all';
$searchQuery = $_GET['search'] ?? '';

// Build query
$sql = "SELECT * FROM users WHERE 1=1";
$params = [];

if ($filterRole !== 'all') {
    $sql .= " AND role = ?";
    $params[] = $filterRole;
}

if ($filterStatus !== 'all') {
    $sql .= " AND status = ?";
    $params[] = $filterStatus;
}

if ($searchQuery) {
    $sql .= " AND (full_name LIKE ? OR email LIKE ? OR phone LIKE ?)";
    $params[] = "%$searchQuery%";
    $params[] = "%$searchQuery%";
    $params[] = "%$searchQuery%";
}

$sql .= " ORDER BY created_at DESC";

$stmt = $pdo->prepare($sql);
$stmt->execute($params);
$users = $stmt->fetchAll();

// Count by role
$roleCounts = [];
foreach(['admin', 'client', 'freelancer'] as $role) {
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM users WHERE role = ?");
    $stmt->execute([$role]);
    $roleCounts[$role] = $stmt->fetch()['count'];
}

$pageTitle = 'Manage Users - Admin';
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

        </form>
    </div>
</div>

<script>
function changeStatus(userId, currentStatus) {
    document.getElementById('modalUserId').value = userId;
    document.querySelector('select[name="status"]').value = currentStatus;
    document.getElementById('statusModal').style.display = 'flex';
}

function closeStatusModal() {
    document.getElementById('statusModal').style.display = 'none';
}

function viewUser(userId) {
    // Redirect to user detail page
    window.location.href = 'user-detail.php?id=' + userId;
}
</script>

<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.3/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

### **FILE 3: admin/services.php**

<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Admin Services Management
 * File: admin/services.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireRole('admin');

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();

// Handle service toggle active
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['toggle_active'])) {
    $serviceId = (int)$_POST['service_id'];
    $newStatus = (int)$_POST['is_active'];
    
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE services SET is_active = ? WHERE service_id = ?");
    if ($stmt->execute([$newStatus, $serviceId])) {
        setFlashMessage('success', 'Service status updated!');
    } else {
        setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to update service!');
    }
    redirect('services.php');
}

// Get all services
$services = getServices([]);

// Group by category
$categories = [];
foreach($services as $service) {
    $categories[$service['category']][] = $service;
}

$pageTitle = 'Manage Services - Admin';
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<style>

<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Client Orders Page
 * File: client/orders.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireLogin();

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Get user orders
$userOrders = getUserOrders($userId);

// Get order detail if ID provided
$orderDetail = null;
$orderItems = [];
if (isset($_GET['id'])) {
    $orderId = (int)$_GET['id'];
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM orders WHERE order_id = ? AND user_id = ?");
    $stmt->execute([$orderId, $userId]);
    $orderDetail = $stmt->fetch();
    
    if ($orderDetail) {
        $orderItems = getOrderItems($orderId);
    }
}

$pageTitle = 'My Orders - ' . SITE_NAME;
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<style>

                        </div>

### **FILE 5: client/payments.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Client Payments Page
 * File: client/payments.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireLogin();

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Handle payment upload
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['upload_payment'])) {
    $orderId = (int)$_POST['order_id'];
    $paymentMethod = cleanInput($_POST['payment_method']);
    $bankName = cleanInput($_POST['bank_name'] ?? '');
    $accountName = cleanInput($_POST['account_name'] ?? '');
    $accountNumber = cleanInput($_POST['account_number'] ?? '');
    $amount = (float)$_POST['amount'];
    
    // Verify order belongs to user
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM orders WHERE order_id = ? AND user_id = ?");
    $stmt->execute([$orderId, $userId]);
    $order = $stmt->fetch();
    
    if (!$order) {
        setFlashMessage('error', 'Invalid order!');
        redirect('payments.php');
    }
    
    // Handle file upload
    if (isset($_FILES['payment_proof']) && $_FILES['payment_proof']['error'] === UPLOAD_ERR_OK) {
        $uploadResult = uploadFile($_FILES['payment_proof'], 'payments');
        
        if ($uploadResult['success']) {
            // Insert payment record
            try {
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                    INSERT INTO payments (order_id, amount, payment_method, payment_proof, bank_name, account_name, account_number, payment_date, status)
                    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, NOW(), 'pending')
                ");
                $stmt->execute([
                    $orderId,
                    $amount,
                    $paymentMethod,
                    $uploadResult['path'],
                    $bankName,
                    $accountName,
                    $accountNumber
                ]);
                
                setFlashMessage('success', 'Payment proof uploaded successfully! Waiting for verification.');
                redirect('orders.php?id=' . $orderId);
                
            } catch (Exception $e) {
                error_log("Payment Upload Error: " . $e->getMessage());
                setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to upload payment. Please try again.');
            }
        } else {
            setFlashMessage('error', $uploadResult['message']);
        }
    } else {
        setFlashMessage('error', 'Please upload payment proof!');
    }
}

// Get pending orders
$stmt = $pdo->prepare("
    SELECT * FROM orders 
    WHERE user_id = ? AND status = 'pending'
    ORDER BY created_at DESC
");
$stmt->execute([$userId]);
$pendingOrders = $stmt->fetchAll();

// Get selected order
$selectedOrder = null;
if (isset($_GET['order'])) {
    $orderId = (int)$_GET['order'];
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM orders WHERE order_id = ? AND user_id = ?");
    $stmt->execute([$orderId, $userId]);
    $selectedOrder = $stmt->fetch();
}

$pageTitle = 'Upload Payment - ' . SITE_NAME;
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<script>
function handleFileSelect(input) {
    const fileUploadArea = document.getElementById('fileUploadArea');
    const fileUploadText = document.getElementById('fileUploadText');
    
    if (input.files && input.files[0]) {
        const file = input.files[0];
        const fileName = file.name;
        const fileSize = (file.size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2); // MB
        
        fileUploadArea.classList.add('has-file');
        fileUploadText.innerHTML = `
            <i class="bi bi-file-earmark-check" style="font-size: 2rem; color: var(--gold);"></i><br>
            <strong>${fileName}</strong><br>
            <small>${fileSize} MB</small>
        `;
    }
}

// Drag and drop
const fileUploadArea = document.getElementById('fileUploadArea');
const paymentProofInput = document.getElementById('paymentProof');

['dragenter', 'dragover', 'dragleave', 'drop'].forEach(eventName => {
    fileUploadArea.addEventListener(eventName, preventDefaults, false);
});

function preventDefaults(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
}

['dragenter', 'dragover'].forEach(eventName => {
    fileUploadArea.addEventListener(eventName, () => {
        fileUploadArea.style.background = 'rgba(255,180,0,0.2)';
    }, false);
});

['dragleave', 'drop'].forEach(eventName => {
    fileUploadArea.addEventListener(eventName, () => {
        fileUploadArea.style.background = '';
    }, false);
});

fileUploadArea.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
    const dt = e.dataTransfer;
    const files = dt.files;
    paymentProofInput.files = files;
    handleFileSelect(paymentProofInput);
}, false);
</script>

<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.3/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>
```

### **FILE 6: client/profile.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Client Profile Page
 * File: client/profile.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireLogin();

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Handle profile update
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['update_profile'])) {
    $fullName = cleanInput($_POST['full_name']);
    $phone = cleanInput($_POST['phone']);
    
    $errors = [];
    
    if (empty($fullName) || strlen($fullName) < 3) {
        $errors[] = 'Name must be at least 3 characters!';
    }
    
    if (!empty($phone) && !isValidPhone($phone)) {
        $errors[] = 'Invalid phone number!';
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE users SET full_name = ?, phone = ? WHERE user_id = ?");
        if ($stmt->execute([$fullName, $phone, $userId])) {
            $_SESSION['user_name'] = $fullName;
            $_SESSION['user_phone'] = $phone;
            setFlashMessage('success', 'Profile updated successfully!');
        } else {
            setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to update profile!');
        }
        redirect('profile.php');
    } else {
        foreach($errors as $error) {
            setFlashMessage('error', $error);
        }
    }
}

// Handle password change
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['change_password'])) {
    $currentPassword = $_POST['current_password'];
    $newPassword = $_POST['new_password'];
    $confirmPassword = $_POST['confirm_password'];
    
    $errors = [];
    
    // Get current user
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT password FROM users WHERE user_id = ?");
    $stmt->execute([$userId]);
    $user = $stmt->fetch();
    
    if (!password_verify($currentPassword, $user['password'])) {
        $errors[] = 'Current password is incorrect!';
    }
    
    $passwordValidation = validatePassword($newPassword);
    if (!$passwordValidation['valid']) {
        $errors[] = $passwordValidation['message'];
    }
    
    if ($newPassword !== $confirmPassword) {
        $errors[] = 'New passwords do not match!';
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        $hashedPassword = password_hash($newPassword, PASSWORD_DEFAULT);
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE users SET password = ? WHERE user_id = ?");
        if ($stmt->execute([$hashedPassword, $userId])) {
            setFlashMessage('success', 'Password changed successfully!');
        } else {
            setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to change password!');
        }
        redirect('profile.php');
    } else {
        foreach($errors as $error) {
            setFlashMessage('error', $error);
        }
    }
}

// Get user data
$currentUser = getCurrentUser();

$pageTitle = 'My Profile - ' . SITE_NAME;
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

                               required>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="col-md-6 mb-3">
                        <label class="form-label text-light">Email</label>
                        <input type="email" 
                               class="form-control form-control-profile" 
                               value="<?php echo htmlspecialchars($currentUser['email']); ?>"
                               disabled>
                        <small class="text-light">Email cannot be changed</small>

                        <label class="form-label text-light">Phone Number</label>
                        <input type="tel" 
                               name="phone" 
                               class="form-control form-control-profile" 
                               value="<?php echo htmlspecialchars($currentUser['phone'] ?? ''); ?>"
                               placeholder="08xxxxxxxxxx">
                    </div>

<script>
function handleFileSelect(input) {
    const fileUploadArea = document.getElementById('fileUploadArea');
    const fileUploadText = document.getElementById('fileUploadText');
    
    if (input.files && input.files[0]) {
        const file = input.files[0];
        const fileName = file.name;
        const fileSize = (file.size / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(2); // MB
        
        fileUploadArea.classList.add('has-file');
        fileUploadText.innerHTML = `
            <i class="bi bi-file-earmark-check" style="font-size: 3rem; color: var(--gold);"></i><br>
            <strong>${fileName}</strong><br>
            <small>Size: ${fileSize} MB</small>
        `;
    }
}

// Drag and drop support
const fileUploadArea = document.getElementById('fileUploadArea');

fileUploadArea.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    fileUploadArea.style.background = 'rgba(255,180,0,0.2)';
});

fileUploadArea.addEventListener('dragleave', (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    fileUploadArea.style.background = '';
});

fileUploadArea.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    fileUploadArea.style.background = '';
    
    const files = e.dataTransfer.files;
    if (files.length > 0) {
        document.getElementById('paymentProof').files = files;
        handleFileSelect(document.getElementById('paymentProof'));
    }
});
</script>

<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.3/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>
```

### **FILE 6: client/profile.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Client Profile Page
 * File: client/profile.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireLogin();

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Get current user data
$currentUser = getCurrentUser();

// Handle profile update
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['update_profile'])) {
    $fullName = cleanInput($_POST['full_name']);
    $phone = cleanInput($_POST['phone']);
    
    $errors = [];
    
    if (empty($fullName) || strlen($fullName) < 3) {
        $errors[] = 'Name must be at least 3 characters!';
    }
    
    if (!empty($phone) && !isValidPhone($phone)) {
        $errors[] = 'Invalid phone number!';
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE users SET full_name = ?, phone = ? WHERE user_id = ?");
        if ($stmt->execute([$fullName, $phone, $userId])) {
            $_SESSION['user_name'] = $fullName;
            setFlashMessage('success', 'Profile updated successfully!');
            redirect('profile.php');
        } else {
            setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to update profile!');
        }
    } else {
        foreach($errors as $error) {
            setFlashMessage('error', $error);
        }
    }
}

// Handle password change
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['change_password'])) {
    $currentPassword = $_POST['current_password'];
    $newPassword = $_POST['new_password'];
    $confirmPassword = $_POST['confirm_password'];
    
    $errors = [];
    
    // Verify current password
    if (!password_verify($currentPassword, $currentUser['password'])) {
        $errors[] = 'Current password is incorrect!';
    }
    
    // Validate new password
    $passwordValidation = validatePassword($newPassword);
    if (!$passwordValidation['valid']) {
        $errors[] = $passwordValidation['message'];
    }
    
    if ($newPassword !== $confirmPassword) {
        $errors[] = 'New passwords do not match!';
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        $hashedPassword = password_hash($newPassword, PASSWORD_DEFAULT);
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE users SET password = ? WHERE user_id = ?");
        if ($stmt->execute([$hashedPassword, $userId])) {
            setFlashMessage('success', 'Password changed successfully!');
            redirect('profile.php');
        } else {
            setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to change password!');
        }
    } else {
        foreach($errors as $error) {
            setFlashMessage('error', $error);
        }
    }
}

$pageTitle = 'My Profile - ' . SITE_NAME;
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

## üì¶ **BATCH TERAKHIR: FREELANCER PAGES (3 Files)**

### **FILE 7: freelance/referrals.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Freelancer Referrals Page
 * File: freelance/referrals.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireRole('freelancer');

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Get current user
$currentUser = getCurrentUser();
$referralCode = $currentUser['referral_code'];

// Get all referrals
$stmt = $pdo->prepare("
    SELECT o.*, u.full_name, u.email
    FROM orders o
    LEFT JOIN users u ON o.user_id = u.user_id
    WHERE o.referral_code = ?
    ORDER BY o.created_at DESC
");
$stmt->execute([$referralCode]);
$referrals = $stmt->fetchAll();

// Calculate stats
$totalReferrals = count($referrals);
$totalSales = array_sum(array_map(fn($r) => $r['final_amount'], array_filter($referrals, fn($r) => in_array($r['status'], ['paid', 'completed']))));
$totalCommission = $totalSales * (COMMISSION_RATE / 100);
$pendingReferrals = count(array_filter($referrals, fn($r) => $r['status'] === 'pending'));
$completedReferrals = count(array_filter($referrals, fn($r) => $r['status'] === 'completed'));

// Generate referral link
$referralLink = SITE_URL . '?ref=' . $referralCode;

$pageTitle = 'My Referrals - Freelancer';
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<style>
body {
    background: var(--bg-dark);
}

.dashboard-wrapper {
    display: flex;
    min-height: 100vh;
}

.sidebar {
    width: 280px;
    background: linear-gradient(135deg, rgba(30,92,153,0.2) 0%, rgba(15,48,87,0.3) 100%);
    border-right: 2px solid rgba(255,180,0,0.2);
    padding: 2rem 0;
    position: fixed;
    height: 100vh;
    overflow-y: auto;
    backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
}

.sidebar-brand {
    padding: 0 1.5rem 2rem;
    text-align: center;
    border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,180,0,0.2);
    margin-bottom: 2rem;
}

.sidebar-brand img {
    width: 80px;
    height: 80px;
    border-radius: 50%;
    border: 3px solid var(--gold);
    margin-bottom: 1rem;
}

.sidebar-menu {
    list-style: none;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
}

.sidebar-menu li a {
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    padding: 1rem 1.5rem;
    color: var(--text-light);
    text-decoration: none;

<script>
function copyReferralLink() {
    const linkInput = document.getElementById('referralLinkInput');
    linkInput.select();
    linkInput.setSelectionRange(0, 99999);
    
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(linkInput.value).then(() => {
        alert('Referral link copied to clipboard!');
    }).catch(err => {
        alert('Failed to copy link');
    });
}
</script>

<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.3/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

### **FILE 8: freelance/commissions.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Freelancer Commissions Page
 * File: freelance/commissions.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireRole('freelancer');

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Get commission records
$stmt = $pdo->prepare("
    SELECT c.*, o.order_number, u.full_name as customer_name
    FROM freelancer_commissions c
    LEFT JOIN orders o ON c.order_id = o.order_id
    LEFT JOIN users u ON o.user_id = u.user_id
    WHERE c.freelancer_id = ?
    ORDER BY c.created_at DESC
");
$stmt->execute([$userId]);
$commissions = $stmt->fetchAll();

// Calculate stats
$totalEarned = 0;
$pendingAmount = 0;
$approvedAmount = 0;
$paidAmount = 0;

foreach($commissions as $commission) {
    $totalEarned += $commission['commission_amount'];
    
    if ($commission['status'] === 'pending') {
        $pendingAmount += $commission['commission_amount'];
    } elseif ($commission['status'] === 'approved') {
        $approvedAmount += $commission['commission_amount'];
    } elseif ($commission['status'] === 'paid') {
        $paidAmount += $commission['commission_amount'];
    }
}

$pageTitle = 'Commissions - Freelancer';
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

### **FILE 9: freelance/withdraw.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Freelancer Withdrawal Page
 * File: freelance/withdraw.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireRole('freelancer');

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Get current user
$currentUser = getCurrentUser();

// Handle withdrawal request
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['request_withdrawal'])) {
    $amount = (float)$_POST['amount'];
    $bankName = cleanInput($_POST['bank_name']);
    $accountNumber = cleanInput($_POST['account_number']);
    $accountName = cleanInput($_POST['account_name']);
    
    $errors = [];
    
    // Validate amount
    if ($amount < MINIMUM_WITHDRAWAL) {
        $errors[] = 'Minimum withdrawal is ' . formatRupiah(MINIMUM_WITHDRAWAL);
    }
    
    // Check available balance
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
        SELECT SUM(commission_amount) as available
        FROM freelancer_commissions
        WHERE freelancer_id = ? AND status = 'approved'
    ");
    $stmt->execute([$userId]);
    $available = $stmt->fetch()['available'] ?? 0;
    
    if ($amount > $available) {
        $errors[] = 'Insufficient balance. Available: ' . formatRupiah($available);
    }
    
    if (empty($bankName) || empty($accountNumber) || empty($accountName)) {
        $errors[] = 'Please fill in all bank details!';
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        try {
            $pdo->beginTransaction();
            
            // Create withdrawal request
            $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                INSERT INTO withdrawal_requests (freelancer_id, amount, bank_name, account_number, account_name, status, requested_at)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 'pending', NOW())
            ");
            $stmt->execute([$userId, $amount, $bankName, $accountNumber, $accountName]);
            
            // Update commission status to 'processing'
            $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                UPDATE freelancer_commissions 
                SET status = 'processing'
                WHERE freelancer_id = ? AND status = 'approved'
                LIMIT ?
            ");
            
            // Calculate how many commissions to mark as processing
            $stmt = $pdo->prepare("
                SELECT commission_id, commission_amount 
                FROM freelancer_commissions
                WHERE freelancer_id = ? AND status = 'approved'
                ORDER BY created_at ASC
            ");
            $stmt->execute([$userId]);
            $approvedCommissions = $stmt->fetchAll();
            
            $remainingAmount = $amount;
            foreach($approvedCommissions as $commission) {
                if ($remainingAmount <= 0) break;
                
                $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE freelancer_commissions SET status = 'processing' WHERE commission_id = ?");
                $stmt->execute([$commission['commission_id']]);
                
                $remainingAmount -= $commission['commission_amount'];
            }
            
            $pdo->commit();
            
            setFlashMessage('success', 'Withdrawal request submitted successfully! Please wait for admin approval.');
            redirect('withdraw.php');
            
        } catch (Exception $e) {
            $pdo->rollBack();
            error_log("Withdrawal Error: " . $e->getMessage());
            setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to process withdrawal. Please try again.');
        }
    } else {
        foreach($errors as $error) {
            setFlashMessage('error', $error);
        }
    }
}

// Get available balance
$stmt = $pdo->prepare("
    SELECT SUM(commission_amount) as available
    FROM freelancer_commissions
    WHERE freelancer_id = ? AND status = 'approved'
");
$stmt->execute([$userId]);
$availableBalance = $stmt->fetch()['available'] ?? 0;

// Get withdrawal history
$stmt = $pdo->prepare("
    SELECT * FROM withdrawal_requests
    WHERE freelancer_id = ?
    ORDER BY requested_at DESC
");
$stmt->execute([$userId]);
$withdrawals = $stmt->fetchAll();

// Calculate stats
$totalWithdrawn = array_sum(array_map(fn($w) => $w['amount'], array_filter($withdrawals, fn($w) => $w['status'] === 'approved')));
$pendingWithdrawals = count(array_filter($withdrawals, fn($w) => $w['status'] === 'pending'));

$pageTitle = 'Withdraw - Freelancer';
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<style>

    background: var(--bg-dark);

### **FILE 1: admin/portfolios.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Admin Portfolio Management
 * File: admin/portfolios.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireRole('admin');

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();

// Handle portfolio toggle featured
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['toggle_featured'])) {
    $portfolioId = (int)$_POST['portfolio_id'];
    $isFeatured = (int)$_POST['is_featured'];
    
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE portfolio SET is_featured = ? WHERE portfolio_id = ?");
    if ($stmt->execute([$isFeatured, $portfolioId])) {
        setFlashMessage('success', 'Portfolio updated successfully!');
    }
    redirect('portfolios.php');
}

// Handle delete portfolio
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['delete_portfolio'])) {
    $portfolioId = (int)$_POST['portfolio_id'];
    
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("DELETE FROM portfolio WHERE portfolio_id = ?");
    if ($stmt->execute([$portfolioId])) {
        setFlashMessage('success', 'Portfolio deleted successfully!');
    } else {
        setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to delete portfolio!');
    }
    redirect('portfolios.php');
}

// Get all portfolios
$portfolios = getPortfolioItems();

// Group by category
$categories = [];
foreach($portfolios as $portfolio) {
    $categories[$portfolio['category']][] = $portfolio;
}

$pageTitle = 'Manage Portfolios - Admin';
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<style>
body {
    background: var(--bg-dark);
}

.dashboard-wrapper {
    display: flex;
    min-height: 100vh;

    padding: 2rem 0;
    position: fixed;
    height: 100vh;
    overflow-y: auto;
    backdrop-filter: blur(10px);
}

    padding: 0 1.5rem 2rem;
    text-align: center;
    border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,180,0,0.2);
    margin-bottom: 2rem;
}

.sidebar-brand img {
    width: 60px;
    height: 60px;
    border-radius: 15px;
    margin-bottom: 0.5rem;
}

.sidebar-menu {
    list-style: none;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
}

.sidebar-menu li a {
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    padding: 1rem 1.5rem;
    color: var(--text-light);
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: all 0.3s;
}

.sidebar-menu li a:hover,
.sidebar-menu li a.active {
    background: rgba(255,180,0,0.1);
    color: var(--gold);
    border-left: 4px solid var(--gold);
}

.sidebar-menu li a i {
    font-size: 1.2rem;
    margin-right: 1rem;
    width: 25px;

### **FILE 2: admin/testimonials.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Admin Testimonials Management
 * File: admin/testimonials.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireRole('admin');

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();

// Handle testimonial approval
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['approve_testimonial'])) {
    $testimonialId = (int)$_POST['testimonial_id'];
    
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE testimonials SET is_approved = 1 WHERE testimonial_id = ?");
    if ($stmt->execute([$testimonialId])) {
        setFlashMessage('success', 'Testimonial approved!');
    }
    redirect('testimonials.php');
}

// Handle testimonial rejection
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['reject_testimonial'])) {
    $testimonialId = (int)$_POST['testimonial_id'];
    
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE testimonials SET is_approved = 0 WHERE testimonial_id = ?");
    if ($stmt->execute([$testimonialId])) {
        setFlashMessage('success', 'Testimonial rejected!');
    }
    redirect('testimonials.php');
}

// Handle delete testimonial
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['delete_testimonial'])) {
    $testimonialId = (int)$_POST['testimonial_id'];
    
    $stmt = $pdo->prepare("DELETE FROM testimonials WHERE testimonial_id = ?");
    if ($stmt->execute([$testimonialId])) {
        setFlashMessage('success', 'Testimonial deleted!');
    }
    redirect('testimonials.php');
}

// Get all testimonials
$stmt = $pdo->query("
    SELECT t.*, u.full_name, u.email 
    FROM testimonials t
    LEFT JOIN users u ON t.user_id = u.user_id
    ORDER BY t.created_at DESC
");
$testimonials = $stmt->fetchAll();

// Count by status
$approved = count(array_filter($testimonials, fn($t) => $t['is_approved'] == 1));
$pending = count(array_filter($testimonials, fn($t) => $t['is_approved'] == 0));

$pageTitle = 'Manage Testimonials - Admin';
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<style>
body {
    background: var(--bg-dark);
}

    display: flex;

}

}

}

    margin-bottom: 0.5rem;
}

    list-style: none;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
}

    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    padding: 1rem 1.5rem;
    color: var(--text-light);
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: all 0.3s;
}

.sidebar-menu li a:hover,
.sidebar-menu li a.active {
    background: rgba(255,180,0,0.1);
    color: var(--gold);
    border-left: 4px solid var(--gold);
}

    font-size: 1.2rem;

            </div>

                <small class="text-light">Pending Approval</small>

            <div class="stat-small">
                <h4 class="text-gold fw-bold mb-1"><?php echo count($testimonials); ?></h4>
                <small class="text-light">Total Reviews</small>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <!-- Testimonials List -->
        <?php if (!empty($testimonials)): ?>
            <?php foreach($testimonials as $testimonial): ?>
            <div class="testimonial-card <?php echo $testimonial['is_approved'] ? '' : 'pending'; ?>">
                <div class="row align-items-center">
                    <div class="col-md-8">
                        <div class="d-flex align-items-center mb-2">
                            <img src="https://ui-avatars.com/api/?name=<?php echo urlencode($testimonial['full_name']); ?>&background=FFB400&color=0F3057&size=50" 
                                 class="rounded-circle me-3" 
                                 width="50" 
                                 height="50">
                            <div>
                                <h5 class="text-gold fw-bold mb-0">
                                    <?php echo htmlspecialchars($testimonial['full_name']); ?>

                                <small class="text-light"><?php echo htmlspecialchars($testimonial['email']); ?></small>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                <?php endif; ?>

                        </small>

### **FILE 4: freelance/profile.php**

```php
<?php
/**
 * =====================================================
 * SITUNEO DIGITAL - Freelancer Profile Page
 * File: freelance/profile.php
 * =====================================================
 */

require_once '../includes/config.php';
require_once '../includes/functions.php';

requireRole('freelancer');

$currentLang = getCurrentLang();
$userId = $_SESSION['user_id'];

// Get current user data
$currentUser = getCurrentUser();

// Handle profile update
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['update_profile'])) {
    $fullName = cleanInput($_POST['full_name']);
    $phone = cleanInput($_POST['phone']);
    
    $errors = [];
    
    if (empty($fullName) || strlen($fullName) < 3) {
        $errors[] = 'Name must be at least 3 characters!';
    }
    
    if (!empty($phone) && !isValidPhone($phone)) {
        $errors[] = 'Invalid phone number!';
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE users SET full_name = ?, phone = ? WHERE user_id = ?");
        if ($stmt->execute([$fullName, $phone, $userId])) {
            $_SESSION['user_name'] = $fullName;
            setFlashMessage('success', 'Profile updated successfully!');
            redirect('profile.php');
        } else {
            setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to update profile!');
        }
    } else {
        foreach($errors as $error) {
            setFlashMessage('error', $error);
        }
    }
}

// Handle password change
if ($_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] === 'POST' && isset($_POST['change_password'])) {
    $currentPassword = $_POST['current_password'];
    $newPassword = $_POST['new_password'];
    $confirmPassword = $_POST['confirm_password'];
    
    $errors = [];
    
    if (!password_verify($currentPassword, $currentUser['password'])) {
        $errors[] = 'Current password is incorrect!';
    }
    
    $passwordValidation = validatePassword($newPassword);
    if (!$passwordValidation['valid']) {
        $errors[] = $passwordValidation['message'];
    }
    
    if ($newPassword !== $confirmPassword) {
        $errors[] = 'New passwords do not match!';
    }
    
    if (empty($errors)) {
        $hashedPassword = password_hash($newPassword, PASSWORD_DEFAULT);
        $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE users SET password = ? WHERE user_id = ?");
        if ($stmt->execute([$hashedPassword, $userId])) {
            setFlashMessage('success', 'Password changed successfully!');
            redirect('profile.php');
        } else {
            setFlashMessage('error', 'Failed to change password!');
        }
    } else {
        foreach($errors as $error) {
            setFlashMessage('error', $error);
        }
    }
}

$pageTitle = 'My Profile - Freelancer';
include '../includes/header.php';
?>

<style>

    <style>

### **FILE 7: .htaccess**

```apache
# =====================================================
# SITUNEO DIGITAL - Apache Configuration
# File: .htaccess
# =====================================================

# Enable Rewrite Engine
RewriteEngine On

# Remove .php extension
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_FILENAME} !-d
RewriteCond %{REQUEST_FILENAME}\.php -f
RewriteRule ^(.*)$ $1.php [L]

# Custom Error Pages
ErrorDocument 404 /errors/404.php
ErrorDocument 500 /errors/500.php

# Security Headers
<IfModule mod_headers.c>
    # Prevent clickjacking
    Header set X-Frame-Options "SAMEORIGIN"
    
    # XSS Protection
    Header set X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block"
    
    # Prevent MIME sniffing
    Header set X-Content-Type-Options "nosniff"
    
    # Referrer Policy
    Header set Referrer-Policy "strict-origin-when-cross-origin"
</IfModule>

# Disable directory browsing
Options -Indexes

# Protect sensitive files
<FilesMatch "^(config\.php|functions\.php|\.env)$">
    Order allow,deny
    Deny from all
</FilesMatch>

# Force HTTPS (uncomment when deploying to production)
# RewriteCond %{HTTPS} off
# RewriteRule ^(.*)$ https://%{HTTP_HOST}%{REQUEST_URI} [L,R=301]

# Compression
<IfModule mod_deflate.c>
    AddOutputFilterByType DEFLATE text/html text/plain text/xml text/css text/javascript application/javascript application/json
</IfModule>

# Browser Caching
<IfModule mod_expires.c>
    ExpiresActive On
    ExpiresByType image/jpg "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType image/jpeg "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType image/gif "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType image/png "access plus 1 year"
    ExpiresByType text/css "access plus 1 month"
    ExpiresByType application/javascript "access plus 1 month"
    ExpiresByType image/x-icon "access plus 1 year"
</IfModule>

# UTF-8 Encoding
AddDefaultCharset UTF-8

# File Upload Limit (adjust as needed)
php_value upload_max_filesize 10M
php_value post_max_size 10M
php_value max_execution_time 300
php_value max_input_time 300
```

## üìÑ **DOCUMENT 1: INSTALLATION_GUIDE.md**

```markdown
# üöÄ SITUNEO DIGITAL - Installation Guide

## System Requirements

### Minimum Requirements:
- **PHP**: 7.4 or higher (8.0+ recommended)
- **MySQL**: 5.7 or higher / MariaDB 10.3+
- **Web Server**: Apache 2.4+ with mod_rewrite enabled
- **Storage**: 500MB minimum
- **RAM**: 512MB minimum

### Recommended Requirements:
- **PHP**: 8.1+
- **MySQL**: 8.0+ / MariaDB 10.6+
- **Web Server**: Apache 2.4+ or Nginx
- **Storage**: 2GB+
- **RAM**: 2GB+
- **SSL Certificate**: For HTTPS

---

## üì• Installation Steps

### Step 1: Download & Extract Files

1. Download the SITUNEO DIGITAL package
2. Extract to your web server directory:
   - cPanel: `public_html/`
   - XAMPP: `htdocs/`
   - Local: Your web root directory

### Step 2: Create Database

#### Using phpMyAdmin:
1. Open phpMyAdmin
2. Click "New" to create database
3. Database name: `situneo_digital`
4. Collation: `utf8mb4_unicode_ci`
5. Click "Create"

#### Using MySQL Command Line:
```sql
CREATE DATABASE situneo_digital CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci;
```

### Step 3: Import Database Schema

1. In phpMyAdmin, select `situneo_digital` database
2. Click "Import" tab
3. Choose file: `database/schema.sql`
4. Click "Go"
5. Wait for import to complete

**‚úÖ Success message should appear!**

### Step 4: Configure Database Connection

1. Open `includes/config.php`
2. Update database credentials:

```php
// Database Configuration
define('DB_HOST', 'localhost');        // Your database host
define('DB_NAME', 'situneo_digital');  // Your database name
define('DB_USER', 'root');             // Your database username
define('DB_PASS', '');                 // Your database password
```

**For cPanel hosting:**
```php
define('DB_HOST', 'localhost');
define('DB_NAME', 'cpanel_user_situneo');
define('DB_USER', 'cpanel_user_dbuser');
define('DB_PASS', 'your_strong_password');
```

### Step 5: Configure Site Settings

In `includes/config.php`, update:

```php
// Site Configuration
define('SITE_NAME', 'Your Company Name');
define('SITE_URL', 'https://yourdomain.com');
define('ADMIN_EMAIL', 'admin@yourdomain.com');

// Contact Information
define('WHATSAPP_NUMBER', '6281234567890');  // Without + or spaces
define('INSTAGRAM_URL', 'https://instagram.com/yourpage');
define('FACEBOOK_URL', 'https://facebook.com/yourpage');
define('LINKEDIN_URL', 'https://linkedin.com/company/yourcompany');

// Bank Account Information
define('BANK_BCA_NUMBER', '1234567890');
define('BANK_BCA_NAME', 'Your Company Name');
define('BANK_MANDIRI_NUMBER', '0987654321');
define('BANK_MANDIRI_NAME', 'Your Company Name');
```

### Step 6: Create Upload Folders

Create these folders with **write permissions (755 or 777)**:

```
uploads/
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ payments/
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ portfolios/
```

**Using cPanel File Manager:**
1. Navigate to `uploads/` folder
2. Right-click ‚Üí "Change Permissions"
3. Set to 755 or 777

**Using FTP/SSH:**
```bash
mkdir -p uploads/payments uploads/portfolios
chmod -R 755 uploads/
```

### Step 7: Configure .htaccess

1. Ensure `.htaccess` exists in root directory
2. For HTTPS (production), uncomment these lines:

```apache
# Force HTTPS
RewriteCond %{HTTPS} off
RewriteRule ^(.*)$ https://%{HTTP_HOST}%{REQUEST_URI} [L,R=301]
```

### Step 8: Test Installation

Visit your website:
```
http://yourdomain.com
```

**‚úÖ You should see the homepage!**

---

- **Email**: `admin@situneo.my.id`
- **Password**: `Situneo2025`

### Demo Client Account:
- **Email**: `budi.santoso@gmail.com`
- **Password**: `Situneo2025`
