---

## üõ†Ô∏è Post-Installation Steps

### 1. Change Admin Password
1. Login as admin
2. Go to Admin ‚Üí Settings
3. Update your password

### 2. Update Site Content
1. **Services**: Go to Admin ‚Üí Services
2. **Portfolio**: Go to Admin ‚Üí Portfolios
3. **Testimonials**: Go to Admin ‚Üí Testimonials

### 3. Configure Email (Optional)
For email notifications, configure SMTP in `includes/config.php`:

```php
// Email Configuration (Optional)
define('SMTP_HOST', 'smtp.gmail.com');
define('SMTP_PORT', 587);
define('SMTP_USER', 'your-email@gmail.com');
define('SMTP_PASS', 'your-app-password');
define('SMTP_FROM', 'noreply@yourdomain.com');
define('SMTP_FROM_NAME', 'SITUNEO DIGITAL');
```

### 4. Setup SSL Certificate (Production)
**Using cPanel:**
1. Go to SSL/TLS
2. Click "Install SSL Certificate"
3. Let's Encrypt is free!

**Using Certbot (VPS):**
```bash
sudo certbot --apache -d yourdomain.com -d www.yourdomain.com
```

### 5. Security Checklist
- [ ] Change all default passwords
- [ ] Set proper file permissions (644 for files, 755 for folders)
- [ ] Disable directory browsing
- [ ] Enable HTTPS
- [ ] Regular backups
- [ ] Keep PHP/MySQL updated

---

## üêõ Troubleshooting

### Issue: "Database connection failed"
**Solution:**
1. Check database credentials in `config.php`
2. Verify database exists
3. Check MySQL service is running
4. Verify database user has proper permissions

### Issue: "404 Not Found" on pages
**Solution:**
1. Check `.htaccess` exists
2. Enable `mod_rewrite` in Apache
3. Restart web server

**Apache:**
```bash
sudo a2enmod rewrite
sudo systemctl restart apache2
```

### Issue: "Permission denied" when uploading files
**Solution:**
1. Set proper permissions on `uploads/` folder:
```bash
chmod -R 755 uploads/
```
2. Check folder ownership
3. Ensure PHP has write access

### Issue: Images not displaying
**Solution:**
1. Check file paths in database
2. Verify upload folder permissions
3. Check `.htaccess` rules

### Issue: "Session errors"
**Solution:**
1. Check PHP session configuration
2. Verify `/tmp` folder has write permissions
3. Clear browser cache and cookies

---

## üîÑ Update & Maintenance

### Regular Backups
**Database:**
```bash
mysqldump -u username -p situneo_digital > backup_$(date +%Y%m%d).sql
```

**Files:**
```bash
tar -czf backup_files_$(date +%Y%m%d).tar.gz /path/to/website
```

### Update Schedule:
- **Daily**: Database backup
- **Weekly**: Full backup (files + database)
- **Monthly**: Security updates & patches

```markdown
# üë§ SITUNEO DIGITAL - Client User Manual

## Table of Contents
1. [Getting Started](#getting-started)
2. [Registration & Login](#registration--login)
3. [Browse Services](#browse-services)
4. [Calculate Price](#calculate-price)
5. [Place Order](#place-order)
6. [Upload Payment](#upload-payment)
7. [Track Order](#track-order)
8. [Manage Profile](#manage-profile)

---

## üöÄ Getting Started

Welcome to SITUNEO DIGITAL! This guide will help you navigate our platform and order digital services.

### What You Can Do:
- ‚úÖ Browse our services and pricing
- ‚úÖ Calculate project costs
- ‚úÖ Place orders
- ‚úÖ Upload payment proof
- ‚úÖ Track order status
- ‚úÖ Manage your profile

---

## üìù Registration & Login

### How to Register:

1. **Visit Registration Page**
   - Click "Register" on navigation bar
   - Or visit: `https://yourdomain.com/auth/register`

2. **Fill Registration Form**
   - **Full Name**: Your complete name
   - **Email**: Valid email address
   - **Phone**: WhatsApp number (format: 08xxxxxxxxxx)
   - **Password**: Minimum 8 characters
   - **Confirm Password**: Must match password
   - **Register As**: Select "Client (Customer)"

3. **Submit**
   - Check "I agree to Terms & Conditions"
   - Click "REGISTER NOW"
   - You'll be logged in automatically!

### How to Login:

1. **Visit Login Page**
   - Click "Login" on navigation bar
   - Or visit: `https://yourdomain.com/auth/login`

2. **Enter Credentials**
   - Email address
   - Password

3. **Login**
   - Check "Remember Me" to stay logged in
   - Click "LOGIN"

**Forgot Password?**
- Click "Forgot Password?" link
- Follow recovery instructions

---

## üõçÔ∏è Browse Services

### View All Services:

1. **Navigate to Services Page**
   - Click "Services" in navigation
   - Or visit: `https://yourdomain.com/services`

2. **Browse by Category**
   - **Website Development**: Company profiles, e-commerce, custom web apps
   - **Mobile Apps**: Android/iOS apps, hybrid apps
   - **Design**: UI/UX, graphic design, branding
   - **Digital Marketing**: SEO, social media, content marketing

3. **View Service Details**
   - Click on any service card
   - See features, pricing, and timeline
   - Click "Order Now" to proceed

---

## üí∞ Calculate Price

### Use Price Calculator:

1. **Go to Calculator Page**
   - Click "Pricing" ‚Üí "Calculator"
   - Or visit: `https://yourdomain.com/calculator`

2. **Select Service Type**
   - Choose from dropdown menu
   - See base price update

3. **Select Features**
   - Check features you need:
     - ‚òëÔ∏è Responsive Design
     - ‚òëÔ∏è Admin Panel
     - ‚òëÔ∏è Payment Gateway
     - ‚òëÔ∏è SEO Optimization
     - And more...

4. **Set Timeline**
   - Urgent (7 days): +50%
   - Normal (14 days): Standard
   - Flexible (30 days): -10%

5. **Enter Referral Code (Optional)**
   - Got a referral code? Get 10% discount!
   - Enter code and click "Apply"

6. **See Final Price**
   - Total cost displayed
   - Breakdown of all charges
   - Click "Order Now" to proceed

---

## üõí Place Order

### Step-by-Step Ordering:

1. **Choose Service**
   - Via Services page, or
   - Via Calculator

2. **Fill Order Details**
   - Project name/description
   - Special requirements
   - Contact information

3. **Review Order**
   - Check all details
   - Verify pricing
   - Add referral code if you have

4. **Submit Order**
   - Click "Place Order"
   - Order number generated
   - Redirected to payment page

**Order Number Format:** `ORD-2025-XXXXX`

---

## üí≥ Upload Payment

### Payment Process:

1. **Go to Payments Page**
   - From dashboard, click "Payments"
   - Or from order confirmation

2. **Select Order to Pay**
   - Choose pending order
   - Click "Pay Now"

3. **See Bank Details**
   - **Bank BCA**: Account number displayed
   - **Bank Mandiri**: Account number displayed
   - Transfer exact amount

4. **Transfer Payment**
   - Use mobile banking/ATM
   - Transfer to our bank account
   - **IMPORTANT**: Transfer exact amount!

5. **Upload Payment Proof**
   - **Payment Method**: Select (Bank Transfer/QRIS/E-wallet)
   - **Bank Name**: Your bank
   - **Account Name**: Your name
   - **Account Number**: Your account number
   - **Upload Screenshot**: Take photo of receipt

6. **Submit**
   - Click "Upload Payment"
   - Wait for admin verification (1-2 hours)
   - You'll receive notification

---

## üì¶ Track Order

### Check Order Status:

1. **Go to My Orders**
   - Dashboard ‚Üí "My Orders"
   - Or: `https://yourdomain.com/client/orders`

2. **View All Orders**
   - See list of all your orders
   - Color-coded status:
     - üü° **Pending**: Waiting for payment
     - üü¢ **Paid**: Payment verified
     - üîµ **In Progress**: Being worked on
     - ‚úÖ **Completed**: Project delivered
     - üî¥ **Cancelled**: Order cancelled

3. **View Order Details**
   - Click "View Details" on any order
   - See complete order information:
     - Order items
     - Payment status
     - Timeline
     - Notes from admin

4. **Order Timeline**
   - Track progress:
     1. Order Created
     2. Payment Confirmed
     3. In Progress
     4. Completed

---

## üë§ Manage Profile

### Update Your Profile:

1. **Go to Profile Page**
   - Dashboard ‚Üí "Profile"
   - Or: `https://yourdomain.com/client/profile`

2. **Edit Information**
   - **Full Name**: Update name
   - **Phone Number**: Update contact
   - **Email**: Cannot be changed

3. **Save Changes**
   - Click "Update Profile"
   - Success message appears

### Change Password:

1. **In Profile Page**
   - Scroll to "Change Password" section

2. **Enter Passwords**
   - **Current Password**: Your old password
   - **New Password**: Minimum 8 characters
   - **Confirm Password**: Must match

3. **Submit**
   - Click "Change Password"
   - Success! You're redirected to login

---

## ‚ùì Frequently Asked Questions

### How long does payment verification take?
**Answer**: Usually 1-2 hours during business hours (9 AM - 5 PM). Outside business hours may take longer.

### Can I cancel my order?
**Answer**: Yes, contact admin via WhatsApp before payment is confirmed. After payment, cancellation depends on project progress.

### How do I use a referral code?
**Answer**: Enter the referral code in the calculator or during order placement. You'll get 10% discount!

### What payment methods are accepted?
**Answer**: Bank transfer (BCA, Mandiri), QRIS, OVO, GoPay. Upload proof after payment.

### When will my project be completed?
**Answer**: Timeline depends on package selected:
- Urgent: 7 days
- Normal: 14 days
- Flexible: 30 days

### Can I request revisions?
**Answer**: Yes! Each project includes revision rounds. Check your service package for details.

## üíº Freelancer Program

### How It Works:

```
1. Register as Freelancer
        ‚Üì
2. Get Unique Referral Code
        ‚Üì
3. Share Your Link
        ‚Üì
4. Customer Orders Using Your Code
        ‚Üì
5. Earn 10% Commission
        ‚Üì
6. Withdraw Earnings
```

### Commission Structure:

| Order Amount | Commission Rate | Your Earnings |
|--------------|-----------------|---------------|
| Rp 1,000,000 | 10% | Rp 100,000 |
| Rp 5,000,000 | 10% | Rp 500,000 |
| Rp 10,000,000 | 10% | Rp 1,000,000 |

**Unlimited earnings potential!** üöÄ

## üîê Your Referral Code

### How to Get Your Code:

1. **Register as Freelancer**
   - Go to: `https://yourdomain.com/auth/register`
   - Select "Freelancer (Referral)"
   - Create custom referral code OR auto-generate
   - Submit registration

2. **View Your Code**
   - Login to dashboard
   - See your code: **`YOURCODE123`**
   - This code is UNIQUE to you!

3. **Referral Link Format**
   ```
   https://yourdomain.com/?ref=YOURCODE123
   ```

### Custom vs Auto-Generated:

**Custom Code:**
- Choose your own (e.g., `JOHN2025`)
- Easy to remember
- Max 20 characters
- Only letters, numbers, and dashes

**Auto-Generated:**
- System creates random code
- Example: `FL7KX9M2`
- Always unique

---

## üì¢ Share Referral Link

### How to Share:

1. **Go to Referrals Page**
   - Dashboard ‚Üí "My Referrals"

2. **Share via Social Media**

   **WhatsApp:**
   ```
   Hi! üëã
   
   Need professional digital services?
   Check out SITUNEO DIGITAL!
   
   ‚úÖ Website Development
   ‚úÖ Mobile Apps
   ‚úÖ Design & Branding
   ‚úÖ Digital Marketing
   
   Use my referral link for 10% discount:
   https://yourdomain.com/?ref=YOURCODE
   
   Questions? Just ask! üòä
   ```

   **Instagram Story:**
   - Screenshot website
   - Add swipe-up link
   - Use engaging caption

   **Facebook Post:**
   - Share services page
   - Add referral link in comments
   - Tag potential clients

   **Telegram:**
   - Share in groups
   - Personal messages
   - Business channels

   - Click Telegram button ‚Üí Auto-share
   - Click Email button ‚Üí Auto-compose

---

## üí∞ Commission System

### How Commissions Work:

1. **Customer Orders**
   - Uses your referral code/link
   - Places order and pays

2. **Commission Status Stages**

   **PENDING** üü°
   - Customer placed order
   - Payment not yet verified
   - You can see it but can't withdraw

   **APPROVED** üü¢
   - Payment verified by admin
   - Order completed
   - Ready to withdraw!

   **PAID** ‚úÖ
   - You requested withdrawal
   - Money transferred to your bank
   - Commission paid out

   **REJECTED** üî¥
   - Order cancelled
   - Payment failed
   - No commission

3. **Commission Calculation**
   ```
   Order Amount: Rp 5,000,000
   Commission Rate: 10%
   Your Earnings: Rp 500,000
   ```

### View Commission History:

1. **Go to Commissions Page**
   - Dashboard ‚Üí "Commissions"

2. **See All Earnings**
   - Total Earned
   - Pending Amount
   - Approved Amount (ready to withdraw)
   - Already Withdrawn

---

## üè¶ Request Withdrawal

### Withdrawal Process:

1. **Check Available Balance**
   - Dashboard shows approved commissions
   - Minimum withdrawal: **Rp 100,000**

2. **Go to Withdraw Page**
   - Dashboard ‚Üí "Withdraw"

3. **Fill Withdrawal Form**
   - **Amount**: Enter amount (max = available balance)
   - **Bank Name**: Select your bank
   - **Account Number**: Your bank account
   - **Account Name**: Account holder name

4. **Submit Request**
   - Click "Request Withdrawal"
   - Request status: PENDING

5. **Wait for Processing**
   - Admin processes within 1-3 business days
   - Money transferred to your account
   - Status changes to: APPROVED

6. **Receive Money**
   - Check your bank account
   - Withdrawal complete!

### Withdrawal Rules:

- ‚úÖ Minimum: Rp 100,000
- ‚úÖ Maximum: Your available balance
- ‚úÖ Processing time: 1-3 business days
- ‚úÖ No withdrawal fees
- ‚úÖ Supported banks: All major Indonesian banks

---

## ‚ùì Frequently Asked Questions

### How do I get paid?
**Answer**: Request withdrawal when you have minimum Rp 100,000 approved commission. Money transferred to your bank account in 1-3 business days.

**Answer**: You earn commission when customer's order is completed and payment verified.

**Answer**: No, referral codes are permanent. Choose wisely during registration!

**Answer**: You only earn commission if customer uses your code/link during ordering.

### Is there a limit to earnings?
**Answer**: No limit! The more you refer, the more you earn.

### Can I be both client and freelancer?
**Answer**: Yes! You can order services AND refer others.

## üì¶ Manage Orders

   - Sidebar ‚Üí "Orders"
   - URL: `https://yourdomain.com/admin/orders`

   - Filter by status (All, Pending, Paid, In Progress, Completed, Cancelled)
   - Search by order number, customer name, or email
   - Sort by date, amount, status

3. **Order Status Meanings**

   | Status | Description | Actions Available |
   |--------|-------------|-------------------|
   | üü° **Pending** | Waiting for payment | Update to Paid/Cancelled |
   | üü¢ **Paid** | Payment verified | Update to In Progress |
   | üîµ **In Progress** | Work in progress | Update to Completed |
   | ‚úÖ **Completed** | Delivered to client | Archive |
   | üî¥ **Cancelled** | Order cancelled | Delete |

### Update Order Status:

1. **Click Order Row**
   - View order details

2. **Change Status**
   - Click "Update Status" button
   - Select new status from dropdown
   - Click "Update"

3. **Status Flow (Recommended)**
   ```
   Pending ‚Üí Paid ‚Üí In Progress ‚Üí Completed
   ```

### View Order Details:

**Order Information:**
- Order Number (ORD-2025-XXXXX)
- Customer name and contact
- Order items with quantities
- Total amount
- Payment status
- Referral code (if used)
- Order notes
- Timeline

**Customer Information:**
- Full name
- Email address
- Phone number
- Previous orders

- Payment method
- Bank details
- Payment proof (if uploaded)
- Transaction date

## üí≥ Process Payments

### Payment Verification:

1. **Navigate to Payments Page**
   - Sidebar ‚Üí "Payments"
   - URL: `https://yourdomain.com/admin/payments`

2. **Pending Payments List**
   - Customer name
   - Order number
   - Amount paid
   - Payment method
   - Bank details
   - Upload date

### Verify Payment:

1. **View Payment Proof**
   - Click "View Proof" button
   - See uploaded screenshot/photo
   - Check payment details

2. **Verify Information**
   - **Amount**: Matches order total?
   - **Bank Account**: Correct destination?
   - **Date**: Recent transaction?
   - **Receipt**: Clear and readable?

3. **Approve Payment**
   - If everything correct:
     - Click "Approve Payment"
     - Order status ‚Üí Paid
     - Customer notified
   
   - If incorrect:
     - Click "Reject Payment"
     - Add rejection reason
     - Customer contacted

### Payment Approval Checklist:

- [ ] Amount matches order total
- [ ] Payment to correct bank account
- [ ] Receipt is clear and readable
- [ ] Transaction date is recent
- [ ] Bank account details match
- [ ] No signs of tampering

---

## üí∏ Process Withdrawals

### Freelancer Withdrawals:

1. **View Withdrawal Requests**
   - Navigate to Freelancers section
   - See pending withdrawal requests

2. **Withdrawal Information**
   - Freelancer name
   - Withdrawal amount
   - Bank details:
     - Bank name
     - Account number
     - Account holder name
   - Request date

3. **Process Withdrawal**

   **Step 1: Verify**
   - Check freelancer has sufficient approved balance
   - Verify bank details
   - Confirm amount

   **Step 2: Transfer**
   - Use internet banking
   - Transfer to freelancer's account
   - Save transaction receipt

   **Step 3: Approve**
   - Click "Approve Withdrawal"
   - Upload transfer proof (optional)
   - Mark as PAID
   - Freelancer notified

4. **Withdrawal Timeline**
   - Request received
   - Verification: Same day
   - Transfer: 1-3 business days
   - Confirmation: After transfer complete

---

## ‚öôÔ∏è System Settings

### Access Settings:

1. **Navigate to Settings Page**
   - Sidebar ‚Üí "Settings"
   - URL: `https://yourdomain.com/admin/settings`

### Settings Sections:

#### 1. General Settings
- Site name
- Site URL
- Admin email
- WhatsApp number
- Social media links

#### 2. Payment Settings
- Bank account information
  - BCA account
  - Mandiri account
- Payment methods accepted
- Payment instructions

#### 3. Commission Settings
- Commission rate (default: 10%)
- Minimum withdrawal amount
- Withdrawal processing time

#### 4. System Information
- PHP version
- Server software
- Database status
- Disk space usage

#### 5. Maintenance
- Clear cache
- Maintenance mode
- Database backup
- System logs

### Update Settings:

**‚ö†Ô∏è Important:**
Most settings are configured in `includes/config.php`

**To Change Settings:**
1. Access server via FTP/cPanel
2. Edit `includes/config.php`
3. Update constants
4. Save file
5. Clear cache

## üìä Reports & Analytics

### Key Metrics:

#### Revenue Analytics:
- **Total Revenue**: All-time earnings
- **Monthly Revenue**: Current month
- **Revenue by Service**: Which services sell most
- **Revenue by Freelancer**: Top referring freelancers

#### Order Analytics:
- **Total Orders**: All-time count
- **Pending Orders**: Require attention
- **Completion Rate**: Orders delivered on time
- **Average Order Value**: Revenue per order

#### User Analytics:
- **Total Clients**: Registered customers
- **Active Clients**: Recent orders
- **Total Freelancers**: Referral partners
- **Active Freelancers**: Recent referrals

### Generate Reports (Manual):

1. **Export Orders**
   - Go to Orders page
   - Select date range
   - Click "Export to Excel/CSV"

2. **Commission Reports**
   - Go to Freelancers page
   - View commission breakdown
   - Export to Excel

3. **Revenue Reports**
   - Dashboard statistics
   - Filter by date range
   - Screenshot or manual calculation

## ‚ùì Admin FAQ

### What if I forget admin password?
**Answer**: Use password recovery or contact system administrator to reset via database.

### How do I add a new admin user?
**Answer**: 
1. Register new account
2. Access database (phpMyAdmin)
3. Update `users` table
4. Set `role = 'admin'`

### Can I customize commission rates per freelancer?
**Answer**: Currently, commission rate is global (10%). Custom rates require code modification.

### How do I handle payment disputes?
**Answer**: 
1. Review payment proof carefully
2. Contact customer via WhatsApp
3. Request additional proof if needed
4. Resolve professionally

### What if freelancer disputes commission?
**Answer**:
1. Check commission calculation
2. Verify order status
3. Review commission policy
4. Communicate clearly

# üõ†Ô∏è SITUNEO DIGITAL - Troubleshooting Guide

## Table of Contents
1. [Common Issues](#common-issues)
2. [Installation Problems](#installation-problems)
3. [Login & Authentication](#login--authentication)
4. [Database Errors](#database-errors)
5. [File Upload Issues](#file-upload-issues)

## üîß Common Issues

### Issue: Website Shows Blank Page

**Symptoms:**
- White/blank page when accessing website
- No error message displayed

**Causes:**
- PHP error with display_errors = Off
- Fatal PHP error
- Memory limit exceeded

**Solutions:**

1. **Enable Error Display**
   ```php
   // Add to top of index.php temporarily
   ini_set('display_errors', 1);
   ini_set('display_startup_errors', 1);
   error_reporting(E_ALL);
   ```

2. **Check Error Logs**
   - cPanel: Error Logs section
   - Server: `/var/log/apache2/error.log`
   - Look for fatal errors

3. **Increase Memory Limit**
   ```php
   // In config.php
   ini_set('memory_limit', '256M');
   ```

4. **Check File Permissions**
   ```bash
   # Files should be 644
   find . -type f -exec chmod 644 {} \;
   
   # Folders should be 755
   find . -type d -exec chmod 755 {} \;
   ```

---

### Issue: "404 Not Found" Error

**Symptoms:**
- All pages except index.php show 404
- URL rewriting not working

**Causes:**
- `.htaccess` not working
- `mod_rewrite` disabled
- Incorrect RewriteBase

**Solutions:**

1. **Check .htaccess Exists**
   ```bash
   ls -la .htaccess
   ```

2. **Enable mod_rewrite (Apache)**
   ```bash
   sudo a2enmod rewrite
   sudo systemctl restart apache2
   ```

3. **Update .htaccess RewriteBase**
   ```apache
   # If site is in subdirectory
   RewriteBase /subdirectory/
   ```

4. **Apache Configuration**
   ```apache
   # In httpd.conf or virtualhost
   <Directory /var/www/html>
       AllowOverride All
   </Directory>
   ```

5. **Test URL Rewriting**
   - Try: `yourdomain.com/about.php` (should work)
   - Try: `yourdomain.com/about` (if 404, rewrite issue)

---

### Issue: Images Not Loading

**Symptoms:**
- Broken image icons
- Portfolio images missing
- Avatar images don't show

**Causes:**
- Incorrect file paths
- Missing uploads folder
- Wrong permissions

**Solutions:**

1. **Check Upload Folders Exist**
   ```bash
   mkdir -p uploads/payments
   mkdir -p uploads/portfolios
   chmod 755 uploads -R
   ```

2. **Verify File Paths**
   ```php
   // Check in database
   SELECT image_url FROM portfolio LIMIT 5;
   
   // Should be like:
   // uploads/portfolios/image.jpg
   ```

3. **Check .htaccess Rules**
   ```apache
   # Make sure this isn't blocking images
   RewriteCond %{REQUEST_FILENAME} !-f
   ```

4. **Set Correct Permissions**
   ```bash
   chmod 755 uploads/
   chmod 644 uploads/portfolios/*
   ```

---

## üîê Login & Authentication

### Issue: Cannot Login as Admin

**Symptoms:**
- "Invalid email or password" error
- Correct credentials not working

**Causes:**
- Database not seeded
- Password hash mismatch
- Account suspended

**Solutions:**

1. **Reset Admin Password via Database**
   ```sql
   -- Access phpMyAdmin
   -- Go to users table
   UPDATE users 
   SET password = '$2y$10$YourNewHashHere',
       status = 'active'
   WHERE email = 'admin@situneo.my.id';
   ```

2. **Generate Password Hash**
   ```php
   <?php
   echo password_hash('Situneo2025', PASSWORD_DEFAULT);
   ?>
   // Copy result and update database
   ```

3. **Check User Status**
   ```sql
   SELECT email, status, role FROM users 
   WHERE email = 'admin@situneo.my.id';
   ```

4. **Verify Database Connection**
   ```php
   // In config.php
   var_dump($pdo); // Should show PDO object
   ```

---

### Issue: "Session Error" Message

**Symptoms:**
- Cannot stay logged in
- Logged out randomly
- Session errors

**Causes:**
- Session folder not writable
- PHP session configuration
- Cookie issues

**Solutions:**

1. **Check Session Path**
   ```php
   <?php
   echo session_save_path();
   // Should show a writable directory
   ?>
   ```

2. **Set Session Path**
   ```php
   // In config.php, before session_start()
   $sessionPath = __DIR__ . '/../sessions';
   if (!is_dir($sessionPath)) {
       mkdir($sessionPath, 0755, true);
   }
   session_save_path($sessionPath);
   ```

3. **Increase Session Lifetime**
   ```php
   // In config.php
   ini_set('session.gc_maxlifetime', 3600); // 1 hour
   session_set_cookie_params(3600);
   ```

4. **Clear Browser Cookies**
   - Chrome: Settings ‚Üí Privacy ‚Üí Clear browsing data
   - Firefox: Options ‚Üí Privacy ‚Üí Clear Data

---

## üíæ Database Errors

### Issue: "Database Connection Failed"

**Symptoms:**
- Cannot connect to database
- "Connection refused" error

**Causes:**
- Incorrect credentials
- MySQL service down
- Database doesn't exist

**Solutions:**

1. **Verify Database Credentials**
   ```php
   // In config.php
   define('DB_HOST', 'localhost');
   define('DB_NAME', 'situneo_digital');
   define('DB_USER', 'your_username');
   define('DB_PASS', 'your_password');
   ```

2. **Test MySQL Connection**
   ```bash
   mysql -u username -p
   # Enter password
   SHOW DATABASES;
   ```

3. **Check MySQL Service**
   ```bash
   # Linux
   sudo systemctl status mysql
   sudo systemctl start mysql
   
   # XAMPP
   # Start MySQL from control panel
   ```

4. **Create Database if Missing**
   ```sql
   CREATE DATABASE situneo_digital 
   CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 
   COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci;
   ```

---

### Issue: "Table Doesn't Exist" Error

**Symptoms:**
- Error: Table 'situneo_digital.users' doesn't exist
- Missing tables

**Causes:**
- Database not imported
- Incorrect database selected
- Table name mismatch

**Solutions:**

1. **Import Database Schema**
   ```bash
   mysql -u username -p situneo_digital < database/schema.sql
   ```

2. **Check Tables Exist**
   ```sql
   USE situneo_digital;
   SHOW TABLES;
   
   -- Should show:
   -- users
   -- services
   -- orders
   -- order_items
   -- etc.
   ```

3. **Re-import Schema**
   - phpMyAdmin ‚Üí Import
   - Select `database/schema.sql`
   - Click Go

---

## üì§ File Upload Issues

### Issue: "Failed to Upload File"

**Symptoms:**
- Payment proof upload fails
- Error message on upload

**Causes:**
- Upload folder not writable
- File size too large
- PHP upload limits

**Solutions:**

1. **Check Folder Permissions**
   ```bash
   chmod 755 uploads/
   chmod 755 uploads/payments/
   chmod 755 uploads/portfolios/
   ```

2. **Increase Upload Limits**
   ```php
   // In .htaccess
   php_value upload_max_filesize 10M
   php_value post_max_size 10M
   php_value max_execution_time 300
   ```

   ```php
   // Or in php.ini
   upload_max_filesize = 10M
   post_max_size = 10M
   max_execution_time = 300
   ```

3. **Check Upload Folder Exists**
   ```php
   <?php
   $uploadDir = 'uploads/payments/';
   if (!is_dir($uploadDir)) {
       mkdir($uploadDir, 0755, true);
   }
   if (!is_writable($uploadDir)) {
       echo "Upload directory not writable!";
   }
   ?>
   ```

4. **Test File Upload**
   ```php
   <?php
   // test-upload.php
   if ($_FILES) {
       var_dump($_FILES);
       var_dump(move_uploaded_file(
           $_FILES['file']['tmp_name'],
           'uploads/test.jpg'
       ));
   }
   ?>
   <form method="post" enctype="multipart/form-data">
       <input type="file" name="file">
       <button type="submit">Test Upload</button>
   </form>
   ```

---

### Issue: "File Type Not Allowed"

**Symptoms:**
- Upload rejected
- "Invalid file type" error

**Causes:**
- File extension validation
- MIME type checking

**Solutions:**

1. **Check Allowed Extensions**
   ```php
   // In functions.php - uploadFile()
   $allowedExtensions = ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'pdf'];
   ```

2. **Add More Extensions**
   ```php
   $allowedExtensions = ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'gif', 'pdf', 'webp'];
   ```

3. **Check File MIME Type**
   ```php
   $finfo = finfo_open(FILEINFO_MIME_TYPE);
   $mimeType = finfo_file($finfo, $_FILES['file']['tmp_name']);
   finfo_close($finfo);
   
   $allowedMimes = [
       'image/jpeg',
       'image/png',
       'image/gif',
       'application/pdf'
   ];
   ```

---

## üí≥ Payment & Orders

### Issue: Payment Status Not Updating

**Symptoms:**
- Order stuck in "Pending"
- Admin approved payment but status unchanged

**Causes:**
- Order update query failed
- Database transaction issue
- Cache problem

**Solutions:**

1. **Manual Status Update**
   ```sql
   -- In phpMyAdmin
   UPDATE orders 
   SET status = 'paid'
   WHERE order_id = 123;
   ```

2. **Check Update Function**
   ```php
   // In admin/orders.php
   $stmt = $pdo->prepare("UPDATE orders SET status = ? WHERE order_id = ?");
   $result = $stmt->execute([$newStatus, $orderId]);
   
   if (!$result) {
       var_dump($stmt->errorInfo());
   }
   ```

3. **Clear Application Cache**
   ```bash
   # If using cache
   rm -rf cache/*
   ```

---

### Issue: Commission Not Calculating

**Symptoms:**
- Freelancer commission shows 0
- Commission table empty

**Causes:**
- Trigger not working
- Commission rate incorrect
- Order not linked to referral

**Solutions:**

1. **Check Referral Code Used**
   ```sql
   SELECT order_id, order_number, referral_code, final_amount
   FROM orders
   WHERE order_id = 123;
   ```

2. **Manually Calculate Commission**
   ```sql
   -- Check if commission record exists
   SELECT * FROM freelancer_commissions
   WHERE order_id = 123;
   
   -- If missing, insert manually
   INSERT INTO freelancer_commissions 
   (order_id, freelancer_id, order_amount, commission_rate, commission_amount, status)
   SELECT 
       o.order_id,
       u.user_id,
       o.final_amount,
       10,
       (o.final_amount * 10 / 100),
       'pending'
   FROM orders o
   JOIN users u ON u.referral_code = o.referral_code
   WHERE o.order_id = 123;
   ```

3. **Verify Commission Rate**
   ```php
   // In config.php
   define('COMMISSION_RATE', 10); // Should be 10%
   ```

---

## ‚ö° Performance Issues

### Issue: Website Loading Slowly

**Symptoms:**
- Pages take 5+ seconds to load
- Database queries slow

**Causes:**
- No database indexes
- Large image files
- No caching
- Shared hosting limits

**Solutions:**

1. **Add Database Indexes**
   ```sql
   -- Add indexes to frequently queried columns
   ALTER TABLE orders ADD INDEX idx_user_id (user_id);
   ALTER TABLE orders ADD INDEX idx_status (status);
   ALTER TABLE orders ADD INDEX idx_created_at (created_at);
   ```

2. **Optimize Images**
   ```bash
   # Use image optimization tools
   # Resize to max 1200px width
   # Compress to 80% quality
   ```

3. **Enable PHP OPcache**
   ```ini
   ; In php.ini
   opcache.enable=1
   opcache.memory_consumption=128
   opcache.max_accelerated_files=10000
   ```

4. **Add Simple Caching**
   ```php
   // Cache database queries
   $cacheFile = 'cache/services.json';
   if (file_exists($cacheFile) && (time() - filemtime($cacheFile) < 3600)) {
       $services = json_decode(file_get_contents($cacheFile), true);
   } else {
       $services = getServices();
       file_put_contents($cacheFile, json_encode($services));
   }
   ```

---

### Issue: High Memory Usage

**Symptoms:**
- "Allowed memory size exhausted" error
- Server running out of RAM

**Causes:**
- Loading too much data
- Memory leaks
- Large file processing

**Solutions:**

1. **Increase Memory Limit**
   ```php
   // In config.php
   ini_set('memory_limit', '256M');
   ```

2. **Paginate Large Queries**
   ```php
   // Instead of loading all orders
   $stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT * FROM orders LIMIT 50");
   
   // Use pagination
   $page = $_GET['page'] ?? 1;
   $perPage = 20;
   $offset = ($page - 1) * $perPage;
   $stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT * FROM orders LIMIT $perPage OFFSET $offset");
   ```

3. **Unset Large Variables**
   ```php
   $largeArray = getAllData();
   // Process data
   unset($largeArray); // Free memory
   ```

---

## üîí Security Concerns

### Issue: SQL Injection Vulnerability

**Symptoms:**
- Suspicious database queries
- Unauthorized data access

**Prevention:**

1. **Always Use Prepared Statements**
   ```php
   // WRONG -


Áî®Êà∑:
Continue

Claude:
```php
 Vulnerable to SQL injection
   $email = $_POST['email'];
   $stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = '$email'");
   
   // CORRECT - Safe from SQL injection
   $email = $_POST['email'];
   $stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = ?");
   $stmt->execute([$email]);
   ```

2. **Validate All Input**
   ```php
   // Use cleanInput() function
   $name = cleanInput($_POST['name']);
   $email = filter_var($_POST['email'], FILTER_VALIDATE_EMAIL);
   ```

3. **Escape Output**
   ```php
   // Always escape when displaying user input
   echo htmlspecialchars($userInput, ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8');
   ```

---

### Issue: XSS (Cross-Site Scripting) Attack

**Symptoms:**
- JavaScript executing in user input
- Malicious scripts in comments/reviews

**Prevention:**

1. **Escape All Output**
   ```php
   // When displaying any user-generated content
   echo htmlspecialchars($content, ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8');
   ```

2. **Sanitize HTML Input**
   ```php
   // If allowing HTML (be careful!)
   $allowed_tags = '<p><a><strong><em><br>';
   $clean = strip_tags($input, $allowed_tags);
   ```

3. **Use Content Security Policy**
   ```php
   // In header.php
   header("Content-Security-Policy: default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://cdn.jsdelivr.net;");
   ```

---

### Issue: Unauthorized File Upload

**Symptoms:**
- PHP files uploaded to server
- Malicious files executed

**Prevention:**

1. **Validate File Types Strictly**
   ```php
   function validateUpload($file) {
       // Check extension
       $allowed = ['jpg', 'jpeg', 'png', 'pdf'];
       $ext = strtolower(pathinfo($file['name'], PATHINFO_EXTENSION));
       
       if (!in_array($ext, $allowed)) {
           return false;
       }
       
       // Check MIME type
       $finfo = finfo_open(FILEINFO_MIME_TYPE);
       $mime = finfo_file($finfo, $file['tmp_name']);
       finfo_close($finfo);
       
       $allowedMimes = [
           'image/jpeg',
           'image/png',
           'application/pdf'
       ];
       
       if (!in_array($mime, $allowedMimes)) {
           return false;
       }
       
       return true;
   }
   ```

2. **Rename Uploaded Files**
   ```php
   // Don't use original filename
   $newFilename = uniqid() . '_' . time() . '.' . $ext;
   ```

3. **Store Outside Web Root**
   ```php
   // Store uploads outside public_html if possible
   $uploadDir = '/home/user/secure_uploads/';
   ```

4. **Disable Script Execution in Upload Folder**
   ```apache
   # In uploads/.htaccess
   php_flag engine off
   AddType text/plain .php .php3 .php4 .php5 .phtml .phar
   ```

---

### Issue: Brute Force Login Attempts

**Symptoms:**
- Multiple failed login attempts
- Server logs show many login tries

**Prevention:**

1. **Implement Rate Limiting**
   ```php
   // In login.php
   session_start();
   
   if (!isset($_SESSION['login_attempts'])) {
       $_SESSION['login_attempts'] = 0;
       $_SESSION['last_attempt'] = time();
   }
   
   // Reset after 15 minutes
   if (time() - $_SESSION['last_attempt'] > 900) {
       $_SESSION['login_attempts'] = 0;
   }
   
   // Check attempts
   if ($_SESSION['login_attempts'] >= 5) {
       $waitTime = 900 - (time() - $_SESSION['last_attempt']);
       die("Too many failed attempts. Try again in " . ceil($waitTime/60) . " minutes.");
   }
   
   // After failed login
   $_SESSION['login_attempts']++;
   $_SESSION['last_attempt'] = time();
   ```

2. **Add CAPTCHA**
   ```html
   <!-- Google reCAPTCHA -->
   <script src="https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js"></script>
   <div class="g-recaptcha" data-sitekey="YOUR_SITE_KEY"></div>
   ```

3. **Log Failed Attempts**
   ```php
   // Log to file
   $logFile = 'logs/failed_logins.txt';
   $logEntry = date('Y-m-d H:i:s') . " - " . $_SERVER['REMOTE_ADDR'] . " - " . $email . "\n";
   file_put_contents($logFile, $logEntry, FILE_APPEND);
   ```

---

## üö® Emergency Procedures

### Emergency: Website Hacked

**Immediate Actions:**

1. **Take Site Offline**
   ```php
   // Create maintenance.php
   <!DOCTYPE html>
   <html>
   <head>
       <title>Under Maintenance</title>
   </head>
   <body>
       <h1>Site Under Maintenance</h1>
       <p>We'll be back soon!</p>
   </body>
   </html>
   ```
   
   ```apache
   # In .htaccess - redirect all traffic
   RewriteEngine On
   RewriteCond %{REQUEST_URI} !^/maintenance\.php$
   RewriteRule ^(.*)$ /maintenance.php [L]
   ```

2. **Change All Passwords**
   - Database password
   - cPanel/hosting password
   - Admin password
   - FTP password

3. **Scan for Malware**
   ```bash
   # Find recently modified PHP files
   find . -name "*.php" -mtime -7 -ls
   
   # Search for suspicious code
   grep -r "eval(" .
   grep -r "base64_decode" .
   grep -r "system(" .
   ```

4. **Check File Integrity**
   ```bash
   # Compare with clean backup
   diff -r /backup/clean/ /current/website/
   ```

5. **Restore from Clean Backup**
   ```bash
   # Backup current (infected) site
   tar -czf infected_backup.tar.gz /path/to/site
   
   # Restore clean backup
   tar -xzf clean_backup.tar.gz
   ```

6. **Update Everything**
   - PHP version
   - Database version
   - All dependencies

---

### Emergency: Database Corrupted

**Symptoms:**
- Tables missing
- Data disappeared
- Database errors everywhere

**Recovery Steps:**

1. **Check Database Status**
   ```sql
   SHOW TABLE STATUS;
   CHECK TABLE users;
   CHECK TABLE orders;
   ```

2. **Repair Tables**
   ```sql
   REPAIR TABLE users;
   REPAIR TABLE orders;
   REPAIR TABLE services;
   ```

3. **Restore from Backup**
   ```bash
   # Stop website first
   
   # Import backup
   mysql -u username -p situneo_digital < backup_20250113.sql
   
   # Verify import
   mysql -u username -p situneo_digital -e "SHOW TABLES;"
   ```

4. **Verify Data Integrity**
   ```sql
   -- Check record counts
   SELECT COUNT(*) FROM users;
   SELECT COUNT(*) FROM orders;
   
   -- Check for NULL values
   SELECT * FROM users WHERE email IS NULL;
   ```

---

### Emergency: Server Down/Unreachable

**Troubleshooting Steps:**

1. **Check Server Status**
   ```bash
   # Ping server
   ping your-server-ip
   
   # Check if web server running
   systemctl status apache2
   systemctl status nginx
   
   # Check if MySQL running
   systemctl status mysql
   ```

2. **Check Server Resources**
   ```bash
   # Check disk space
   df -h
   
   # Check memory
   free -m
   
   # Check CPU
   top
   ```

3. **Check Error Logs**
   ```bash
   # Apache logs
   tail -f /var/log/apache2/error.log
   
   # MySQL logs
   tail -f /var/log/mysql/error.log
   
   # PHP logs
   tail -f /var/log/php/error.log
   ```

4. **Restart Services**
   ```bash
   # Restart Apache
   sudo systemctl restart apache2
   
   # Restart MySQL
   sudo systemctl restart mysql
   
   # Restart PHP-FPM (if using)
   sudo systemctl restart php7.4-fpm
   ```

---

## üìù Logging & Debugging

### Enable Debug Mode:

```php
// In config.php - ONLY for development!
define('DEBUG_MODE', true);

if (DEBUG_MODE) {
    ini_set('display_errors', 1);
    ini_set('display_startup_errors', 1);
    error_reporting(E_ALL);
} else {
    ini_set('display_errors', 0);
    error_reporting(E_ALL & ~E_NOTICE & ~E_DEPRECATED);
}
```

### Custom Error Logging:

```php
// In functions.php
function logError($message, $context = []) {
    $logFile = __DIR__ . '/../logs/error.log';
    $timestamp = date('Y-m-d H:i:s');
    $contextStr = !empty($context) ? json_encode($context) : '';
    $logEntry = "[$timestamp] $message $contextStr\n";
    
    // Create logs folder if not exists
    $logDir = dirname($logFile);
    if (!is_dir($logDir)) {
        mkdir($logDir, 0755, true);
    }
    
    file_put_contents($logFile, $logEntry, FILE_APPEND);
}

// Usage
logError('Order creation failed', ['user_id' => 123, 'order_data' => $orderData]);
```

### Debug Database Queries:

```php
// In functions.php
function debugQuery($stmt) {
    if (DEBUG_MODE) {
        ob_start();
        $stmt->debugDumpParams();
        $debug = ob_get_clean();
        logError('SQL Debug', ['query' => $debug]);
    }
}

// Usage
$stmt = $pdo->prepare("SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = ?");
$stmt->execute([$email]);
debugQuery($stmt);
```

---

## üîç Useful Debugging Tools

### Check PHP Configuration:

```php
<?php
// Create phpinfo.php (DELETE after viewing!)
phpinfo();
?>
```

### Test Database Connection:

```php
<?php
// test-db.php
require_once 'includes/config.php';

try {
    echo "Database connection successful!\n";
    
    $stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM users");
    $result = $stmt->fetch();
    echo "Total users: " . $result['count'] . "\n";
    
    $stmt = $pdo->query("SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM orders");
    $result = $stmt->fetch();
    echo "Total orders: " . $result['count'] . "\n";
    
} catch (Exception $e) {
    echo "Database error: " . $e->getMessage();
}
?>
```

### Check File Permissions:

```bash
# Create check-permissions.sh
#!/bin/bash

echo "Checking file permissions..."
echo ""

echo "Config file:"
ls -l includes/config.php

echo ""
echo "Upload directories:"
ls -ld uploads/
ls -ld uploads/payments/
ls -ld uploads/portfolios/

echo ""
echo "Logs directory:"
ls -ld logs/ 2>/dev/null || echo "Logs directory doesn't exist"
```

‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
Payment Method:      [Bank Transfer ‚ñº]
Bank Name:          [BCA ‚ñº]
Account Name:       [Your Name]
Account Number:     [Your Account No]
Upload Proof:       [Choose File] üì∑
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
```

**Taking Good Payment Proof Screenshot:**
```
‚úÖ GOOD Screenshot:
- Clear and readable
- Shows transaction details
- Shows amount transferred
- Shows destination account
- Shows transaction date/time
- No blur or cut-off

‚ùå BAD Screenshot:
- Blurry image
- Information cut off
- Wrong transaction shown
- Edited or tampered
```

**Step 5: Submit Payment**
```
1. Review all information
2. Click "Upload Payment"
3. See success message
4. Wait for admin verification (1-2 hours)
```

**‚úÖ AFTER UPLOAD:**
- Order status: Pending ‚Üí Awaiting Verification
- You'll receive notification when approved
- Check email/WhatsApp for updates

**Question 1:** What information do you need to register?
```
a) Only email
b) Email and password only
c) Full name, email, phone, and password
d) Just your name
```

**Question 2:** How do you apply a referral code for discount?
```
a) Enter during registration
b) Enter in price calculator
c) Enter during order placement
d) All of the above
```

**Question 3:** What's the correct way to upload payment proof?
```
a) Any photo from gallery
b) Clear screenshot showing transaction details
c) Edited image
d) Text description
```

**Question 4:** How long does payment verification usually take?
```
a) 24 hours
b) 1 week
c) 1-2 hours during business hours
d) Instantly
```

**Question 5:** What status means your project is being worked on?
```
a) Pending
b) Paid
c) In Progress
d) Completed
```

**ANSWERS:** 1-C, 2-D, 3-B, 4-C, 5-C

**Score:**
- 5/5: Excellent! You're ready!
- 3-4/5: Good! Review some sections
- 0-2/5: Please review training again

## üéØ LESSON 1: Freelancer Program Basics (30 minutes)

### **1.1 Understanding the Program**

**What is SITUNEO Freelancer Program?**
```
‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê

‚îÇ                                     ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  Unlimited earning potential        ‚îÇ

‚îÇ  Flexible schedule                  ‚îÇ
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò
```

**How It Works:**
```
STEP 1: REGISTER
‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Get unique referral code

STEP 2: SHARE
‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Share your referral link

STEP 3: CUSTOMER ORDERS
‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Using your code

STEP 4: EARN COMMISSION
‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí 10% of order value

STEP 5: WITHDRAW
‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Transfer to your bank
```

**Commission Structure:**
```
ORDER VALUE          COMMISSION (10%)      YOUR EARNINGS
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
Rp 1,000,000         10%                   Rp 100,000
Rp 2,500,000         10%                   Rp 250,000
Rp 5,000,000         10%                   Rp 500,000
Rp 10,000,000        10%                   Rp 1,000,000
Rp 50,000,000        10%                   Rp 5,000,000
```

**Real Example:**
```
Your Friend: "Saya mau buat website e-commerce"
You: "Pakai SITUNEO DIGITAL aja! Saya kasih link referral"

Friend orders: Rp 7,500,000

Friend orders lagi: Rp 3,000,000

Total dari 1 teman: Rp 1,050,000! üí∞

**Step 1: Navigate to Registration**
```

2. Click "Register" button
```

**Step 2: Fill Registration Form**
```
REGISTRATION FORM
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
Full Name:           [Your complete name]
Email:               [Valid email]
Phone:               [WhatsApp number]
Password:            [Minimum 8 characters]
Confirm Password:    [Same as password]
Register As:         ‚úì Freelancer (Referral) ‚Üê SELECT THIS
Referral Code:       [Custom or leave blank]
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
‚òë I agree to Terms & Conditions
[REGISTER NOW]
```

**Step 3: Create Your Referral Code**

**Option A: Custom Code**
```
‚úÖ GOOD Codes:
- JOHN2025
- BUDIJKT
- MARKETINGPRO
- WEBDESIGNER

‚ùå BAD Codes:
- aaa123 (too generic)
- xxxxxxxxx (hard to remember)
- !!@@## (special chars not allowed)
```

**Tips for Good Referral Code:**
- Your name + year (BUDI2025)
- Your brand (WEBSTUDIO)
- Your niche (DESIGNPRO)
- Easy to remember
- Professional looking
- Max 20 characters

**Option B: Auto-Generated**
```
System creates: FL7KX9M2
- Always unique
- No duplicates
- Use if unsure
```

**Step 4: Complete Registration**
```
1. Check "I agree to Terms"
2. Click "REGISTER NOW"
3. Logged in automatically!
4. See your referral code displayed
```

**‚úÖ CHECKPOINT:**
You should now have:
- ‚úì Freelancer account created
- ‚úì Unique referral code
- ‚úì Access to freelancer dashboard

## üéØ LESSON 2: Referral System Mastery (45 minutes)

### **2.1 Understanding Your Referral Link**

**Your Referral Link Structure:**
```
https://situneo.my.id/?ref=YOURCODE123
        ‚îÇ                    ‚îÇ
        ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ Domain          ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ Your Code
```

**How It Works:**
```
1. Customer clicks your link
   ‚îî‚Üí Referral code saved in browser

2. Customer browses website
   ‚îî‚Üí Code remains active

3. Customer places order
   ‚îî‚Üí Your code automatically applied

4. Order completed & paid
   ‚îî‚Üí Commission credited to you!
```

**Link Tracking:**
```
Your Link: situneo.my.id/?ref=BUDI2025

When customer clicks:
‚úì Cookie stored (30 days)
‚úì Code pre-filled in order form
‚úì Attribution tracked
‚úì Commission calculated
```

---

### **2.2 Getting Your Referral Link**

**EXERCISE 3: Copy Your Referral Link**

**Method 1: From Dashboard**
```
1. Go to Dashboard
2. See "Your Referral Link" section
3. Click "COPY LINK" button
4. Link copied to clipboard!
5. Paste anywhere to share
```

**Method 2: From Referrals Page**
```
1. Navigate to "My Referrals"
2. Top section shows referral link
3. Input field with your link
4. Click "Copy" button
```

**Method 3: Manual Construction**
```
Base URL: https://yourdomain.com
Add: ?ref=
Add: YOURCODE

Result: https://yourdomain.com/?ref=YOURCODE
```

**‚úÖ PRACTICE:**
- Copy your referral link 3 different ways
- Paste in notepad to verify
- Share with yourself on WhatsApp (test)

---

### **2.3 Referral Link Best Practices**

**DO's ‚úÖ**
```
‚úÖ Use shortened links for social media
   bit.ly/situneo-budi
   
‚úÖ Add UTM parameters for tracking
   ?ref=BUDI2025&source=instagram
   
‚úÖ Create QR codes for offline
   [QR Code Generator]
   
‚úÖ Test link before sharing
   Click it yourself first
```

**DON'Ts ‚ùå**
```
‚ùå Spam in random groups
‚ùå Use misleading descriptions
‚ùå Pretend you're not affiliate
‚ùå Share without context
```

**Link Shortening:**
```
Long Link:
https://situneo.my.id/?ref=BUDI2025

Shortened:
bit.ly/situneo-budi
  ‚Üì
Easier to share
Professional looking
Trackable
```

## üéØ LESSON 4: Commission Tracking (30 minutes)

### **4.1 Understanding Commission Status**

**Commission Lifecycle:**
```
PENDING üü°
‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Customer placed order
    ‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Waiting for payment verification
        
APPROVED üü¢
‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Payment verified
    ‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Order completed
        ‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Ready to withdraw!
        
PAID ‚úÖ
‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Withdrawal processed
    ‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Money in your bank account
        
REJECTED üî¥
‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Order cancelled
    ‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí Payment failed
        ‚îî‚îÄ‚Üí No commission earned
```

**Timeline Example:**
```
DAY 1:
10:00 AM - Customer clicks your link
11:30 AM - Customer places order (Rp 5M)
Status: PENDING
Your commission: Rp 500K (pending)

DAY 1:
02:00 PM - Customer uploads payment
03:00 PM - Admin verifies payment
Status: APPROVED
Your commission: Rp 500K (ready to withdraw!)

DAY 3:
09:00 AM - You request withdrawal
Status: PROCESSING

DAY 5:
11:00 AM - Money transferred
Status: PAID
Your commission: Rp 500K (in your bank!) üí∞
```

---

### **4.3 Commission Calculations**

**EXERCISE 8: Calculate Your Earnings**

**Basic Formula:**
```
Commission = Order Amount √ó 10%

Examples:
Rp 1,000,000 √ó 10% = Rp 100,000
Rp 5,000,000 √ó 10% = Rp 500,000
Rp 10,000,000 √ó 10% = Rp 1,000,000
```

**Real Scenario:**
```
YOUR MONTHLY REFERRALS:
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
Week 1: 2 orders (Rp 3M + Rp 5M) = Rp 8M
Week 2: 3 orders (Rp 2M + Rp 4M + Rp 3M) = Rp 9M
Week 3: 1 order (Rp 7M) = Rp 7M
Week 4: 2 orders (Rp 2.5M + Rp 3.5M) = Rp 6M
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
TOTAL: 8 orders = Rp 30M
YOUR COMMISSION: Rp 3M (10%)
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
```

**Income Calculator:**
```
IF you refer 5 orders/month:
Average order: Rp 4M
Monthly sales: Rp 20M
YOUR INCOME: Rp 2M/month

IF you refer 10 orders/month:
Average order: Rp 4M
Monthly sales: Rp 40M
YOUR INCOME: Rp 4M/month

IF you refer 20 orders/month:
Average order: Rp 4M
Monthly sales: Rp 80M
YOUR INCOME: Rp 8M/month üöÄ
```

**‚úÖ PRACTICE CALCULATION:**
```
Calculate commission for:
1. Order Rp 2,750,000 = ?
2. Order Rp 6,500,000 = ?
3. Order Rp 12,000,000 = ?
4. Total 3 orders = ?

ANSWERS:
1. Rp 275,000
2. Rp 650,000
3. Rp 1,200,000
4. Rp 2,125,000
```

## üéØ LESSON 5: Withdrawal Process (15 minutes)

### **4.4 Requesting Withdrawal**

**EXERCISE 9: Make Your First Withdrawal**

**Prerequisites:**
```
‚úì Minimum balance: Rp 100,000
‚úì Commission status: APPROVED
‚úì Bank account ready

```

**Step 1: Check Available Balance**
```
Dashboard shows:
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ

Rp 2,500,000
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
```

**Step 2: Go to Withdraw Page**

```

**Step 3: Fill Withdrawal Form**
```
WITHDRAWAL REQUEST
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
Amount (IDR):        [2500000]
  Min: Rp 100,000
  Max: Rp 2,500,000 (your balance)

Bank Name:           [BCA ‚ñº]
  Options: BCA, Mandiri, BNI, BRI, etc.

Account Number:      [1234567890]
  Your bank account number

Account Name:        [Your Name]
  Must match ID card

‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
‚ö†Ô∏è Make sure bank details are correct!
   
[REQUEST WITHDRAWAL]
```

**Step 4: Submit Request**
```
1. Review all information
2. Click "Request Withdrawal"
3. See confirmation message
4. Status: PENDING
```

**Step 5: Wait for Processing**
```
PROCESSING TIME:
‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
Business Days: 1-3 days
Weekends/Holidays: Next business day

You'll receive:
‚úì Email confirmation
‚úì WhatsApp notification (optional)
‚úì Dashboard status update
```

**Step 6: Receive Money**
```
Once APPROVED:
1. Money transferred to your bank
2. Status changes to: PAID
3. You receive transfer notification
4. Check your bank account! üí∞
```

**‚úÖ WITHDRAWAL CHECKLIST:**
- [ ] Balance ‚â• Rp 100,000
- [ ] Bank account verified
- [ ] Correct account number
- [ ] Account name matches
- [ ] Amount within limit
- [ ] Request submitted

---

### **4.5 Withdrawal Best Practices**

**DO's ‚úÖ**
```
‚úÖ Withdraw regularly (monthly)
‚úÖ Keep bank details updated
‚úÖ Double-check account number
‚úÖ Wait for approval before spending
‚úÖ Keep records of withdrawals
```

**DON'Ts ‚ùå**
```
‚ùå Withdraw before commission approved
‚ùå Use wrong bank account
‚ùå Request multiple times for same amount
‚ùå Expect instant transfer
‚ùå Ignore verification requests
```

**Troubleshooting:**
```
PROBLEM: Withdrawal rejected
SOLUTION: Check bank details, resubmit

PROBLEM: Delayed processing
SOLUTION: Contact admin via WhatsApp

PROBLEM: Wrong amount received
SOLUTION: Send transfer receipt to admin

PROBLEM: Account mismatch
SOLUTION: Update profile with correct info
```

**Question 1:** What is the commission rate for referrals?
```
a) 5%
b) 10%
c) 15%
d) 20%
```

```
a) When customer clicks your link
b) When customer registers
c) When order is placed
d) When order is completed and paid
```

**Question 3:** What's the minimum withdrawal amount?
```
a) Rp 50,000
b) Rp 100,000
c) Rp 500,000
d) Rp 1,000,000
```

**Question 4:** What's the best approach to sharing?
```
a) Spam in every group
b) Provide value first, then share
c) Only share link without context
d) Hide that you're affiliate
```

**Question 5:** How long does withdrawal processing take?
```
a) Instant
b) 1 hour
c) 1-3 business days
d) 1 week
```

**Question 6:** What commission status means ready to withdraw?
```
a) Pending
b) Approved
c) Processing
d) Rejected
```

**Question 7:** Best way to track referrals?
```
a) Guess from memory
b) Check dashboard regularly
c) Ask admin manually
d) Don't track
```

**Question 8:** How to create effective share content?
```
a) Copy-paste same message everywhere
b) Customize for each platform/audience
c) Only share link
d) No need for content
```

**ANSWERS:** 
1-B, 2-D, 3-B, 4-B, 5-C, 6-B, 7-B, 8-B

**Score Interpretation:**
- 8/8: EXCELLENT! Master Freelancer! üèÜ
- 6-7/8: GOOD! Ready to start earning! üí™

- 0-3/8: NEEDS WORK! Retake training üîÑ

## üí¨ FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS

### **General Questions**

**Q: Do I need to pay to join?**
```
A: NO! Freelancer program is 100% FREE.
   No registration fees, no monthly fees.
   You only earn commissions.
```

**Q: Can I be both client and freelancer?**
```
A: YES! You can order services AND
   earn commissions from referrals.
```

**Q: Is there a limit to how much I can earn?**
```
A: NO LIMIT! The more you refer,
   the more you earn. Unlimited potential.
```

**Q: Can I use my own referral code?**
```
A: NO. You cannot earn commission
   from your own orders.
```

---

### **Commission Questions**

**Q: When exactly do I earn commission?**
```
A: Commission credited when:
   1. Customer uses your code
   2. Order is placed
   3. Payment is verified
   4. Order is completed
   
   Status changes to APPROVED
```

**Q: What if customer doesn't use my code?**
```
A: No commission earned.
   Always remind customers to use
   your referral code/link.
```

**Q: Can commission be cancelled?**
```
A: YES, if:
   - Order is cancelled
   - Payment fails
   - Fraud detected
   
   Status changes to REJECTED
```

**Q: How is commission calculated?**
```
A: Simple formula:
   Order Amount √ó 10% = Your Commission
   
   Example:
   Rp 5,000,000 √ó 10% = Rp 500,000
```

---

### **Withdrawal Questions**

**Q: How long before I can withdraw?**
```
A: Once commission is APPROVED,
   you can withdraw immediately.
   
   No waiting period!
```

**Q: What's the minimum withdrawal?**
```
A: Rp 100,000 (one hundred thousand rupiah)
```

**Q: Are there withdrawal fees?**
```
A: NO FEES! You receive 100% of
   your commission.
```

**Q: How long does transfer take?**
```
A: 1-3 business days after approval.
   Weekends/holidays may take longer.
```

**Q: Can I withdraw to any bank?**
```
A: YES! All major Indonesian banks:
   BCA, Mandiri, BNI, BRI, CIMB,
   Permata, Danamon, etc.
```

---

### **Technical Questions**

**Q: How does the referral link work?**
```
A: When customer clicks your link:
   1. Cookie saved (30 days)
   2. Code pre-filled in forms
   3. Attribution tracked
   4. Commission credited to you
```

**Q: What if customer clears cookies?**
```
A: Remind them to manually enter
   your referral code when ordering.
```

**Q: Can I share link on paid ads?**
```
A: YES! You can use:
   - Google Ads
   - Facebook Ads
   - Instagram Ads
   
   At your own cost.
```

**Q: Can I have multiple referral codes?**
```
A: NO. One unique code per freelancer.
   This ensures proper tracking.
```
